Suppressing Bandits: Sichuan Army's Deng and Tian Hesitate and Don't Advance

—Bandit Suppression Support Association Cables Urging Dispatch of Troops—

Chengdu Dispatch: Recently, the military operations of the 3rd, 4th, and 5th Route Armies in suppressing bandits have made great progress. The 5th Route Army has successively recovered Xuanhan and Suiding, and the 4th Route Army under Yang Sen has also recaptured Yingpeng. However, the 1st and 2nd Route Armies under Deng and Tian are still hesitant and not advancing, which greatly hinders the suppression of the Red Army. The Sichuan Bandit Suppression People's Support Association yesterday (the 20th) specifically sent a cable urging the two Commanders Deng and Tian to quickly advance and cut off the bandits' retreat to achieve the effect of encirclement and suppression. The Pacification Committee, on the 18th, jointly sent a circular telegram to various armies, severely criticizing those who were unwilling to seriously and quickly suppress the bandits. Furthermore, the An Chuan Bandit Suppression Promotion Association and others also sent a cable to Xiang and other generals on the 20th, making representations. The various telegrams are recorded below:

Telegram to Deng and Tian: Urgent to Commanders Deng in Zhaohua and Guangyuan, and Commander Tian of Sichuan: According to reports, Commander Tian’s telegram stated that because the 1st Route Army did not take over the Zhaoguang defense, the 2nd Route Army could not move to the right. The true situation is difficult to fathom. We have just received the good news that Xuanhan and Suiding have been successively recovered, and the bandit army is fleeing in panic. We urge you to take advantage of the situation to advance and cut off the bandits’ retreat to achieve the effect of encirclement and suppression. The safety of the situation in Sichuan hinges on this one action. The situation is urgent. Please act quickly. This is respectfully telegraphed for your consideration and reply. Sichuan Bandit Suppression People's Support Association bows.

Telegram from the Pacification Committee: (Above omitted) In the past two months, the main force of the bandits has been concentrated in the lower eastern areas. First Xuanhan and Suiding, then Yingpeng. Our army has repeatedly engaged in battle, bravely resisting the enemy. The areas previously lost have gradually been recovered. If all the armies can advance simultaneously and attack the bandits, then Zhaoguang, Jian, Min, Cangyi, Nan, and other counties would have long been cleared. According to investigations, some use the militia as the vanguard while the army stays in the rear; some soldiers stubbornly guard the rivers while the generals leisurely stay in the cities; some raise funds in peacetime, claiming to be running several state-owned enterprises, but once it comes to suppressing bandits, they use the transfer or retention of a small number of troops to procrastinate and shift responsibility to each other. In summary, the situation is regrettable. Now the bloody battles in Suiding and Xuanhan have started again. Regardless of which army, if they continue to harbor selfish motives, allow the bandits to run rampant, and act perfunctorily, unwilling to seriously and quickly suppress the bandits, then the people of Sichuan have awakened and are no longer afraid to speak out and blame. If they are truly as afraid of the bandits as of tigers, that would be shameful. Or if they harbor bandits to increase their own importance... The proverb says, "Honest advice is unpleasant to the ear but benefits conduct." We offer our sincere advice and hope you will understand. Pacification Committee bows.

Telegram to Liu Xiang: Commander-in-Chief Liu Xiang in Chengdu (remaining titles omitted), and others: As the Red bandits have fled to Sichuan, the northeast has fallen, the dead are stacked like pillows, and the living are displaced. In the past seven or eight months, the bad news has been spreading, and terror has been increasing. You were ordered to suppress the bandits and dispatched six routes of troops. Earlier, we received the good news of the victory at Kaijiang, and the entire occupied area was recovered. The hearts of the people of Sichuan were greatly gladdened. If each route took advantage of the victory to attack in separate directions, how difficult would it be to wipe them out in one fell swoop? But now it has been more than a month. Recent reports indicate that some armies are only thirty to fifty li away from the bandits at the front line but have not launched a single fierce attack. A long night invites dreams; this is truly alarming. The Red bandits, with their newly arrived forces, have seized more than a dozen counties. Each day they occupy strengthens their grip and further anesthetizes the hearts of some of the people. The firmer their base, the more difficult it becomes to attack. This is a clear and obvious principle. Now the armies are slow to advance, claiming to be consolidating their positions, but Jiangxi has been disturbed for several years. Can Sichuan withstand such a long-term disturbance? Furthermore, if this goes on for too long, the Red bandits will grow stronger. In the event that they exploit our weakness and break through at one point, those of you who are far away will be unable to provide timely rescue. If one route collapses, all routes will flee. In the past, the armies of the nine military governors were defeated at Hebei, and the forces of the seven states were turned back at Hangu Pass. Comparing the past with the present, is there any difference? When we think of this, can we even ask about the situation in Sichuan? Moreover, today's grain prices are so low that the income from a year's rent is not enough to pay the pre-collected taxes. The countryside has already gone bankrupt. Although four million yuan was raised earlier, it is still difficult to collect now. If the bandits are not pacified for a long time and taxes are levied again, the disaster of the roving bandits in the late Ming Dynasty will likely spread throughout Sichuan, which will be even more severe than the Red bandits. What is worrying is that some push forward while others retreat, some look ahead while others look back. The rumors flying around seem to have some basis. Your ancestors' graves are located here. If this great disaster is pacified early, the homeland will depend on it. We earnestly hope that you will unite and work together to advance fiercely. We can't help but look forward to this. These are urgent words, so please understand. Chengdu Bandit Suppression An Chuan Promotion Association, Provisional Public Security Maintenance Association, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and various people bow.

Zhang Yitang Breaks Away from the Third Party

Zhang Was a Central Committee Member of the Third Party

Declares the Fujian Incident is Ultimately Doomed to Failure

Hankou Dispatch: Zhang Yitang, a member of the Central Committee of the Third Party, was one of the responsible leaders in the Central Committee. The Workers' and Peasants' Party, which evolved from the Third Party, was initiated and organized by Zhang, and he was also the drafter of its declaration. After Deng Yanda was arrested, he traveled to Qin and Lu to engage in activities. When Li Shucheng was the Director of the Hubei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, he was introduced to Hubei and appointed as the Director of the Provincial Relief Institute, a position he held until today. Prior to this, during the large-scale arrest of reactionaries due to the Fujian Incident, Zhang was also arrested and interrogated by the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital. He confessed the errors in his political line and issued a declaration renouncing the party. The original text is as follows: "Compatriots, comrades, in order to revive the revolution and liberate the nation, I once worked hard and struggled diligently for the Third Party, participated in the First Central Committee of the Third Party, and worked in the Propaganda Committee. However, the facts of several years have completely disappointed me. First, Tan Pingshan and Deng Yanda competed for leadership, using all means of instigation, alienation, deception, and exclusion. Second, under the slogan of the so-called anti-rectification movement, bureaucratic politicians, bandits, and warlords—in short, as long as they could disrupt order, disturb the local area, and resist the central government, regardless of their role for the country and the nation, they were all colluded with as much as possible. Third, in theory, they stood between the Three Principles of the People and Marxism, fully demonstrating their contradictory and wavering heart. In order to correct these errors, I worked hard to study and fought fiercely with Tan Pingshan and others, organizing the Workers' and Peasants' Party, and I drafted the program. However, under the current circumstances in our country, the Workers' and Peasants' Party has no way out and is no different from the Chinese Revolutionary Party. To maintain its existence, it also depends on warlords. The more so-called thorough its thinking, the more it objectively becomes an appendage of the Communist Party. Comrades, the struggle between revolution and counter-revolution has already come to close quarters. The movements of the Third Party, the Workers' and Peasants' Party, and the Social Democratic Party can only serve to please the Communist Party, deceive young people, split the country, and disrupt society. Looking at the Fujian Incident this time, at a time when the world is criticizing our country for being disorganized, the rebels openly changed the era name and formed a government to resist the central government. At a time when internal and external troubles are pressing and unity and peace are needed, the rebels do not hesitate to fight a civil war by colluding with the Communist Party for the sake of the rights of a few. Is this not a violent act of destroying the nation and ruining the country? Those with even a little conscience, how could they bear to do this? The Fujian rebels fantasize about replaying the story of the alliance with the Communist Party to overthrow the central government, but they have forgotten the lessons of the February Revolution in Russia and the failure of the Social Revolutionary Party, especially the tragedies of the riots in the two Lakes and Guangzhou in the fifteenth and sixteenth years [of the Republic, 1926 and 1927]. The Fujian rebels attempt to use ambitious military men, but the seizure of fire by ambitious military men born of the concept of power and territory will become a head-on blow to them. The rebels dream even more of uniting various parties to increase their strength, but in the history of world political movements, experience proves that the complexity within Fujian and its sharp struggles are strong facts that will inevitably lead to failure. As for the rebels' weak military strength, financial difficulties, and the poverty of the local area, etc., these are especially their fatal crises. Therefore, the Fujian rebellion, besides failure, only serves to strengthen the enemy, prolong internal strife, lose international credibility, and even provoke opportunism and attacks from imperialists. In other words, the Fujian rebellion will only further fragment the country and endanger the nation. Comrades, compatriots, there is only one path to national revival: that is, spiritual unity, strengthening the central government, strengthening national power, and striving to resist foreign aggression. This great and arduous mission can only be accomplished under the banner of the Three Principles of the People, which has a long history and brilliant brilliance. Hesitating young people, comrades, the moment of life and death for the nation has arrived. Time does not allow for a moment's hesitation. Immediately return to the ranks of the Three Principles of the People! Former Central Committee Member of the First Chinese Revolutionary Party, Zhang Yitang." (26th)

Poison Manufacturing Facility Cracked in Huanggang County, Hubei Province

Extremely Large Scale, with Morphine as the Main Product

Four Criminals Arrested, All Stolen Goods Sent to the Province

Hankou Dispatch: A large-scale poison manufacturing facility was cracked in Sujiazu, Huanggang County, at the beginning of this month. Four criminals have been arrested successively, and all the stolen goods were escorted to the province on the 26th, and the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs immediately submitted them to the Provincial Government for review and instructions on how to handle them. Previously, the head of the joint defense in Yangluo Town discovered several unfamiliar people in Xindian Township on the 4th of this month, living together in a secluded house, acting suspiciously. He reported this to the Sixth District Chief Zhu Yi, who led the district guards to conduct a secret investigation, but there were no signs. When they investigated the Sujiazu area on the lakeside connected to the 261st and 262nd Bao [group of households] , they saw a large secluded house, where several people dressed in modern style clothing, aged about twenty or thirty, were working behind the house. Suspecting them of being rebels, they returned to the district and ordered Tao Jiankui, the head of the joint defense in Yangluo Town, to dispatch district guards and Ding [local order-keepers] to search the area at dawn on the 5th. They cracked this large-scale poison manufacturing facility. However, the main criminals had already fled upon hearing the news. Three people, namely the chief steward Sun Xinwei, Zhang Jinhong, and Jiang Wanlou, were arrested on the spot. Subsequently, the main criminal Yuan Jinzhang was also arrested. They were all sent to the county government. County Magistrate Zhu Baosan immediately detained Sun and others and ordered the seized machinery and drugs to be escorted to the prefecture for inventory and storage. At the same time, he telegraphed the Provincial Government and the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions. The Department of Civil Affairs, upon receiving the report, considered the case to be serious and immediately telegraphed County Magistrate Zhu to send someone to escort them to the province for investigation and handling. He dispatched Zhu Yi, the Chief of the Sixth District, and Wang Shu and Wan Guohua, officials from the county government, along with twenty armed soldiers from the security team, to escort all the machinery and drugs to the province on the 26th, where they were handed over to the Department of Civil Affairs for inventory and safekeeping. The Department of Civil Affairs sent the drugs and raw materials to the Provincial Hospital for testing. The results showed that only a small portion contained narcotics, while the rest were raw materials for manufacturing morphine. The four criminals who were arrested are still being held in the county, awaiting interrogation. Meng Guangpeng, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, has approved three items: (1) Commend and reward those who contributed to the cracking of the case, with the funds to be advanced from the anti-smoking income; (2) Interrogate and handle the criminals in accordance with the regulations for investigating and banning narcotic drugs; (3) Seal up the seized raw materials with their original markings and submit them to the Provincial Government for review and instructions on how to handle them. The poison manufacturing machinery will be displayed in a selected location for public viewing. (26th)

Rampant Bandits in Runan

The 8th District Security Team Suffers Defeat in Suppression

Over a Hundred Officers and Soldiers Killed, Two Hundred Guns Lost

Kaifeng Dispatch: The bandit gangs of Huo Guodong and Yang Xiaohei in Yu [Henan] province are running rampant in the eastern and southern counties of Henan, burning and looting dozens of villages and killing countless people. Although the authorities have repeatedly sent troops to suppress them, when there are many soldiers, the bandits turn large gangs into small groups to evade capture; when there are few soldiers, they unite their forces to resist, hoping to seize weapons. According to a person from Runan, on the 18th of this month, Chen Bojia, the Commander of the 8th District Security Force, sent his chief of staff Yang Zengkui to lead one company each from the security forces of Xiping, Suiping, Zhengyang, and Shangcai counties, three companies from Runan County, and one platoon from Queshan County, totaling more than 600 men, to search and suppress the remaining bandits in the area bordering Runan and Xiangcheng, including Damazhuang, Mitosi, and Sheqiao. They captured more than 20 people along the way and seized dozens of guns. When they arrived near Yangbu, they received a report from Xincai County that more than 2,000 bandits from the gangs of Huo Guodong, Yang Xiaohei, Li Furen, and Zhang Xueliang were fleeing towards Runan. They immediately dispatched troops to intercept them. Unexpectedly, the bandits' plainclothes sentries had already reached the east gate of Yangbu, intending to attack the officers and soldiers from the rear. After being discovered, they immediately divided their troops to drive them back. Then the bandits launched a large-scale attack. The officers and soldiers fought bravely, engaging in hand-to-hand combat with the bandits several times. Staff Officer Yang, realizing that the enemy outnumbered them, ordered the Suiping Security Team to bypass and attack the bandits from the rear, launching a surprise attack from both sides. However, the bandits launched a fierce cavalry charge, counter-attacking to the rear of the officers and soldiers. As a result, more than 600 men were surrounded. They relied on a desperate breakout and temporarily retreated to Yangbu Stockade to hold firm. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already infiltrated the stockade and colluded with the local ruffians, creating disturbances and causing chaos. Gunfire broke out everywhere, and the order was disrupted. The bandits outside the stockade took the opportunity to launch a fierce attack. Yang Zengkui was killed by a bullet during the internal and external attacks. With no one in command, the troops scattered. Hu Jiwu, the captain of the Runan Security Company, led more than a dozen soldiers to hold a blockhouse to the death. Eventually, because it was difficult to support the building alone, they were captured and killed. In this battle, the losses included Staff Officer Yang Zengkui, Captain Hu Jiwu, and several other officers, more than thirty soldiers killed, several officers, including Li Chunguan, and several dozen soldiers captured, and several officers, including Liao Xiangfan, and dozens of soldiers seriously wounded, for a total loss of about 200 guns. It is said that the bandits also suffered heavy casualties. On the 20th, Liu Fengqi's 13th Cavalry Brigade and Liu Huixin's Brigade of the 11th Route rushed to the scene. The bandits began to flee to the territory of Taihe County in Anhui Province. (December 24th)

Shandong's Notorious Bandit Wang Ziming Captured

—Executed by Firing Squad After Interrogation—

Jinan Dispatch: Wang Ziming, a notorious bandit in eastern Shandong, had hundreds of men under his command. He roamed through Zhucheng, Anqiu, Linqu, and Shangmi for seven or eight years, as famous and ruthless as Zhang Heilian in southern Shandong. The people of eastern Shandong watched him with fear. In the past two years, due to the vigorous bandit suppression efforts by the local troops and militias in the province, large and small bandit gangs have been wiped out one after another. Wang Zhiqi, Hao Mingzhu, and others have all been brought to justice. A reward of 10,000 yuan was offered for Wang Ziming's capture. Wang, realizing that it was difficult to operate, came to Jinan to lie low. His younger brother, Wang Huideng, is currently a martial arts instructor at the Provincial National Martial Arts Institute. Wang Ziming relied on his brother and lived at No. 147 Jushan Street, near the Jinde Association. Liu Yaoting, the captain of the special service team, sent detective He Zhenshan to track and investigate. After confirming the information, at 9:00 AM yesterday (the 24th), he led a team of officers, three female police officers from the Public Security Bureau, and officers from the local Public Security Sub-bureau to surround and arrest Wang at the address. Wang Ziming, his younger brother Wang Huideng, his mother Wang Yuan, his sister Wang Huilan, his wife Wang Li, his young daughter Xiao Ni, Wang Huideng's wife Wang Dai, his young son Wang Jiafu, Wang’s servant Wang Dezhen, and the landlord Qiao Cai were all taken into custody. 5,800 yuan in cash and several thousand yuan worth of gold and jade jewelry were found hidden in the women's trousers. They were all taken to the military law office. This morning (the 25th), Shi Jingzhou, the director of the military law office, interrogated them at the military law office. According to Wang Ziming's confession, he is 38 years old, from Fuliu Village, 50 li north of Zhucheng. There are three brothers. My brother Wang Youdeng is dead. My third brother, Wang Huideng, is now in custody. Wang Li is my woman, and I have a boy and my younger siblings. I was first kidnapped to be a bandit. Afterwards, I sought to turn in my guns to avoid death but could not. I had no choice but to continue until now. I have been a bandit for seven or eight years. There are still more than 200 men under my command, led by Zhou Zhiting, Hu Desheng, and Lin Shigang. I don't know where they are now. In the 19th year [of the Republic, 1930], I was introduced by Ge Zhisheng of Wang Village in Gaomi to surrender to Zhang Buyun (i.e., the Lian Zhuang Association of the 8th District of Gaomi). Ge defrauded me of 22 guns. I have no people, no guns, and no savings in Jinan. If the Chairman employs me, I can gather them and surrender." Wang Huideng confessed that he is 25 years old, graduated from the former Martial Arts Training Institute, and worked as a former staff member for Director Zhang at the National Martial Arts Institute. He is currently a teacher at the National Martial Arts Institute and has not been involved in banditry. (He Zhenshan testified that Wang Huideng did not follow his brother in banditry.) Wang Yuan confessed that she is 65 years old and Wang Ziming is her son from her first marriage. He left home nine years ago. Wang Li confessed that she is 28 years old, from Shilitun north of Yidu, and was forced to marry Wang Ziming more than ten years ago. She has a little girl named Xiao Ni. Wang Dai confessed that she is 30 years old, from Yidu County. Wang Huideng is my husband, and Wang Ziming is my brother. He came here in July. My husband advised him to leave, but he wouldn't listen. My husband went to Nanjing. The money I brought was given to me by my sister-in-law. In addition, the servant Wang Dezhen and the landlord Qiao Cai confessed that they did not know that Wang Ziming was a bandit. After the questioning was completed, Shi Jingzhou, the director of the military law office, reported to Han Fuqu [the governor of Shandong]. Han ordered that Wang, having been captured, should be executed immediately to appease the people. Therefore, at 1:30 PM, a car took Wang Ziming to Luokou in the north of the city to be executed by firing squad. The notorious bandit of many years was brought to justice in one day, and the people were very happy. His younger brother, Wang Huideng, and the rest of his family are still being held. If ordinary people harbor bandits, they should be punished accordingly. Wang Huideng is Wang Ziming's brother, so it is understandable that he did not report him. The investigation is still ongoing. If it is confirmed that Huideng did not follow his brother in banditry, he will be released. The reward of 10,000 yuan will be awarded to He Zhenshan, the lead investigator in this case, and the female police officers of the special service team. As for Liu Yaoting, the captain of the special service team, he is currently in Jiaodong capturing the remaining bandits. Only a few of Wang’s bandit underlings escaped. It is said that there are still twenty or thirty bandits in Pingdu, Shandong, appearing and disappearing from time to time. It is expected that they will all be cleared up soon. (25th)

Inspection Notes of Gan, Wan, Xiang and E Provinces (By our special correspondent, Ren An)

The Rural Situation of Susong and Taihu

Taihu Correspondence: Entering Anhui from Huangmei, the first stop is Susong. The two places are only forty li apart, and the rural situations are largely the same. Rent must also be paid in advance. Even for the best land, rent must be paid. Land is relatively concentrated, with several households in the county renting from 5,000 to 10,000 dan. The area is near rivers and lakes and prone to flooding. The China International Famine Relief Commission operates a credit cooperative there, with an annual interest rate of 4%. Members are limited to farmers easily affected by floods, and the purpose seems to be solely to provide relief for floods. The custom of foot binding for women is very prevalent, and there are many who have not yet unbound their feet, especially in the countryside. Although smoking and gambling are ostensibly strictly prohibited, many secretly violate the rules.

The county seat was once occupied by bandits for three weeks, and wealthy households and gentry suffered significant losses. Later, they were driven back by the national army, and both the city and countryside were able to return to normal. Many public officials in local self-government organs have contracted bad habits. They do not distinguish between public and private interests in terms of economics, and they often shirk their responsibilities in public affairs, leading to the successive county magistrates' planned construction projects becoming empty talk on paper. For example, the construction of dikes over the years has involved huge sums of money, but the yearly floods are still unavoidable. The officials in charge are irresponsible, and even corrupt. When villagers occasionally discuss this, they all curse vehemently. The rural economy is extremely depleted. The currency circulating in the market and surrounding villages is mostly paper money issued by merchants. The issuance of this paper money is unrestricted. Any merchant, even restaurants and teahouses, can issue it freely. The post office refuses to accept it, but others are surrounded by the environment and have no choice but to accept it reluctantly. Magistrate Tao wants to rectify the financial situation and wants to ban these paper money, but he cannot realize it because of the financial depression. Money houses cannot use credit for foreign exchanges, but must use cash, and the number of foreign exchanges is increasing more than before, which is also an abnormal phenomenon.

The county's rice production is insufficient in normal years, relying on about 20,000 shi imported from neighboring counties. Miscellaneous grains and wheat are exported, about 80,000 to 100,000 shi, and are sold to Jiujiang, Zhenjiang, Shanghai, and other places. Special products include riverside melon seeds, lakeside silver fish, and the tobacco industry, which are all renowned in the world.

Heading north to Taihu County, the Anhui First District Commissioner's Office is located there. It is said that the Commissioner has not been in office for long, and he is quite serious about banning smoking. Notices of execution for offenders are posted in the four cities, so there are no people who openly smoke. It seems to be a good scene. However, when he first took office, he brought too many people and could not place them. Just when the smoking ban was strict, he widely appointed them to inspect smoking offenders. But there are unscrupulous elements among them who secretly carry smoking devices for inspection. If they encounter honest and easily deceived families, even if there is no criminal behavior, they will bring out the smoking devices they carry, falsely accuse them as evidence, and extort money. The people suffer greatly from this. Fortunately, the realization came early, and the harm is still shallow.

The county government was once in urgent need of government expenses and issued a kind of "receipt" (meaning bond), divided into one yuan, two yuan, three yuan, and five yuan, which were purchased in advance by grain households with cash, and could be used for grain payment in the autumn. When the autumn levy began, the county government used cash shortage as an excuse, and issued a notice to the levy office that "receipts" for grain payment would only be accepted for half, and the remaining half would still be collected in cash. Grain households had no choice but to comply. However, the "receipts" they held were all in whole amounts and could not be exchanged for change. When they asked the levy office for change, they were told that the county government had no cash and refused to give any. Fearing that they would be fined for exceeding the deadline, they prepared the full amount of cash and paid on time. Unexpectedly, rumors suddenly spread that the "receipts" would soon expire. At the same time, merchants willing to buy "receipts" at a discount emerged. Most of the grain households holding "receipts" were ignorant villagers, who were troubled by the uselessness of the "receipts". Suddenly hearing the news that they could be sold, they all rushed to sell them at lower prices, not even caring about the huge losses they suffered. However, these merchants dared to buy these "receipts" so suddenly, and there was naturally something special about it.

Very few farmers in various villages are self-cultivating, and most are tenant farmers. The tenant farming methods are: one is to pay a deposit (i.e., rent deposit), called "Baozhuang"; the other is not to pay, called "Qingzhuang". The amount of the deposit is not fixed, generally 20 to 30 yuan per shi of land. The right to sublet exists in Baozhuang, but not in Qingzhuang. The amount of rent paid is mostly determined temporarily. The usual ratio between the landlord and tenant is four to six for Baozhuang, and six to four for Qingzhuang. If a tenant wants to leave, if it is Qingzhuang, they can do so casually. If it is Baozhuang, the landlord must first propose it, and there must be a special reason to return the entire deposit and obtain the tenant's consent before it can be done. Otherwise, if the tenant has no arrears, they have the right to continue farming. In places that were disturbed by the communists a few years ago, the rent amount has been appropriately reduced. Even the old "three-tenths rent", which was even heavier than "landlord six, tenant four", is now reduced to "eighteen percent deduction" or even "fifteen percent deduction" (the so-called three-tenths rent means that if the harvest is three shi, the landlord gets two shi and the tenant gets one shi. The so-called fifteen percent deduction or eighteen percent deduction means that the two shi is reduced to one shi and five dou or one shi and eight dou, which are all local terms). Five years ago, the price of one mu of land was 80 yuan for the best, and 40 yuan for the second. Now the best has fallen to 40 yuan, and the medium and low have also fallen by half. The wages of hired laborers are about 30 to 40 yuan per year, which is roughly the same as in other places, but in this place, clothes, shoes, hats, and tobacco money are provided, which seems to be better than in other places. All other spiritual treatments are more progressive than before. It is said that these phenomena all occurred after the communist disturbances.

The annual production of rice can generally be self-sufficient. Usually, because the wheat produced is mostly transported to Shipai, Anqing, and other places, the rice from Qianjiang and Jiangxi can be transported in to supplement it, about 200,000 to 300,000 shi per year. There are also poria cocos, lacquer, hide oil, chestnuts, silver fish, tea, persimmons, and pears, etc., with an annual output value of 300,000 to 400,000 yuan. Also, coming here from Susong, the white mountains are rugged, all of which are limestone. Limestone is produced nearby, especially in Xueshan'ao.

The counties of Huoshan, Luan, and Lihuang to the north are all destinations to be inspected. However, going directly to Huoshan from here is 380 li, passing through the mountains of Wanshan (i.e., Tianzhu Mountain) and the Fenjieling Mountains. There are still small groups of communist Red Guards who appear from time to time. If they encounter public officials or wealthy merchants, their heads will not be safe. Moreover, remote villagers secretly hide firearms. Whenever they see passersby, if there is an opportunity, they will also transform into bandits and loot their silver and goods. However, they do not let go of the poor and do not tie up the rich, which is different from the Red Army. Therefore, the traffic on this road has long been cut off invisibly, so the route has been changed. It is planned to take a boat from Xujiadu, cross the lake, arrive at Anqing, transfer to a car and pass through Tongcheng and other counties, and go to Luan.

Huangpu Port Construction Plan

Planned to be constructed in four phases, step by step

To be completed within fifty years

Guangzhou Correspondence: The plan for the construction of Huangpu Port in Guangdong has been advocated for a long time, but it has not been implemented due to financial constraints. However, the port development plan has been designed and surveyed by Chinese and foreign engineers sent by the Guangdong River Management Committee for several times. Recently, the River Management Committee has brought up the old topic again and sent technician Li to prepare a Huangpu Port construction plan, which was submitted to the Standing Committee of the River Management Committee and submitted to the Southwest Political Affairs Conference for review. According to the construction procedures planned this time, it is divided into four phases and implemented in phases. The first phase is to establish the prototype of Huangpu Port, which is planned to be completed in five years. The second phase is to develop Huangpu Port into a third-class port and a commercial port, which is planned to be completed in ten years. The third phase is to develop Huangpu into a second-class port and a small city, which is planned to be completed in fifteen years. The fourth phase is to complete Huangpu as a first-class port and a large city, which is planned to be completed in twenty years. The first phase of the project is planned to build a steel bridge pile embankment of 4,200 feet from the east of Yuzhu Market to the south of Yuchun Fort in front of Xieshan, Zhugang Village, Yuzhu Fort, and Niutouzui, and build six warehouses to form the prototype of a commercial port. The second phase of the project is to maintain the current import waterway of Huangpu, with a depth of 20 feet below the low water level of the spring tide. Ships with a draft of 18 feet can sail at any time, and those with a draft of 23 feet to 25.25 feet can enter when the tide rises. Build shops, set up markets, and open port industrial areas in the port for trade and transportation. The third phase is to develop Huangpu Port into a world-class second-class port and a small city, and deepen the depth of the import waterway to 27 feet below the low water level of the spring tide (excavate approximately 7,924,000 cubic meters of mud) so that ships with a draft of 28 feet to 35.25 feet can enter when the tide rises. Develop port industrial areas, residential areas, small commercial areas, large commercial areas, light industrial areas, heavy industrial areas, and port city administrative areas in the port, and build railways to connect with the Yuehan Railway, and build embankments, warehouses, wharves, and shipyards to form a complete port city. (December 21)

Henan Provincial Government Resolves to Relocate Disaster Victims from Hua County

First, relocate 25,000 people

To various counties along the Pinghan Railway

Kaifeng Correspondence: This summer, the Yellow River breached at Changyuan, and Hua County in northern Henan suffered extremely heavy damage. Now it is the severe winter season, and the water surface is still more than thirty li wide, and its momentum has become a torrent. Recently, it has continued to rise more than three feet, and the huge waves are monstrous, which is even worse than before. Disaster victims in the disaster area, risking danger in boats, go to the shelters in the cities and towns to avoid freezing and starvation. Boats sink, and several occur every day. In mid-November, when Liu Zhi inspected the county, he believed that the Yellow River would not change its course from there, and after the water receded, it would all become sand dunes, and it would be impossible to cultivate. Therefore, he had the idea of ​​moving the disaster victims to the special zone in southern Henan, so that the desolate land that had been repeatedly destroyed by the Red Army would gradually prosper. He also telegraphed the Secretariat of the Provincial Government to convene a meeting of various departments to formulate an implementation plan. It was then drafted by the Henan Relief Committee and submitted to the Provincial Government for review. The Provincial Government ordered the departments of civil affairs, finance, and education to review the original plan and submit it. It advocated first immigrating 50,000 people, but the special zone was almost completely destroyed. If they were moved there, housing, farm tools, cattle, and horses would all need to be prepared, and it would be useless without millions of yuan. It is not easy to raise funds in the provincial treasury. Therefore, the Provincial Government decided at its 309th meeting yesterday to first move 20,000 people to the counties along the Pinghan Railway between Zhangde and Yancheng. During the relocation period, each person will be issued a living allowance of one jiao per day, and children will be issued five fen. The funds will be raised by the Finance Department. After arriving at the designated location, the local government will be responsible for raising everything and finding ways to resettle them. As soon as the preparations are completed, the relocation will begin. As for the plan to relocate to the special zone, it may be shelved indefinitely.

Also, the Shanghai Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association has decided to allocate 30,000 sets of cotton clothes for women and children in the province. The former group telegraphed the group yesterday to unload 8,500 sets at Daokou Railway in northern Henan when transporting to Henan, 2,000 sets on the north bank of the Yellow River, 6,000 sets in Lanfeng, 4,000 sets in Kaifeng, 5,500 sets in Sishui, 1,700 sets in Luoyang, 1,800 sets in Zhengzhou, and 500 sets in Shaan County for distribution. (20th)

Songjiang

Extension of Loaned Grain Repayment for One Year

Previously, this province, due to the provincial treasury's deficit and insufficient income, borrowed grain from the people with the approval of the Finance Department to meet the needs of the province. It was originally scheduled to be repaid the following year, but the number of harvests has been weak for years, and only borrowing has not been repaid. Various counties have repeatedly requested repayment on record. It is heard that the Finance Department initially planned to start this year to repay the funds borrowed since the 18th year in five years, repaying 9 jiao each year and repaying it in full in five years. However, the Finance Department stated that the amount to be repaid each year would be more than 1.2 million, and admitted that since the flood and the Shanghai war, the provincial treasury's income has not been able to cover its expenditures, resulting in the original repayment plan ultimately becoming a mere formality. Therefore, a notice was issued to various counties to inform them that all repayments of borrowed grain will be extended for one year.

Violent Robbers Loot Tax Collection Cash

A wealthy Qu family in Xiyang, near Tianma Mountain, moved to Songjiang in the past and lived east of Ta Bridge. The day before yesterday evening, after the tax collection ended, a violent robber suddenly broke into the accounting room, pulled out a pistol, and forced them to hand over more than 2,000 yuan of tax money, which he took away. Before leaving, he also forced the victim to pretend to be a relative and escort him to the door, where he got into a car and left.

Jiading

Where Did the Abandoned Remains in Front of the County Party Headquarters Come From?

On the afternoon of the 26th, a child from Jiangbei was picking firewood in the open space on the east side in front of the County Party Headquarters. In the discarded grain of the Liao family, a corpse was found, with the flesh inside the skin completely rotten. The head and upper limbs had separated from the torso, and the lower legs below the knees were also missing. Zhang Jinda, the city police officer of Gongliu Tu in charge, reported to the County Public Security Bureau, who forwarded the report to the County Government. County Magistrate Feng, accompanied by trial officer Shao Ling, led the police officers to inspect the body at 11:00 a.m. today. After careful inspection, it was determined to be a male corpse, but since only the bones remained, whether there were any injuries could not be identified. Zhang Jinda, the city police officer, was summoned for questioning. According to his confession, he had no idea where the bones came from. County Magistrate Feng ordered the body to be temporarily buried by Cunrentang and await investigation.

Robbery in Nanxiang South Market at Dusk

In Gaojia Chang Temple in Nanxiang South Market, at dusk on the 20th, a temple keeper, A, was cooking when four robbers suddenly came, pretending to be pilgrims. After entering the room, two guarded the door, and two pulled out bayonets, threatening them to be silent. They rummaged through boxes and cabinets and robbed 15 yuan in cash and 200 copper coins before leaving with a whoop.

Nanhui

The Case of the Robbery of Hua Junchao's Family

At Hua Junchao's home in Hengmian Town, Sixth District of the county, on the night of December 23, many robbers suddenly came, first entering the old lady's room, tying her up with ropes, and forbidding her to make a sound. It is estimated that more than 200 yuan in cash and more than ten pieces of leather clothing were robbed. Then they entered Mrs. Kui Bai's room, searching for all the gold jewelry. They kept asking for cash, about 4,000 yuan. Finally, they entered Mr. Kui Bai's room, taking all his savings over the years. The total loss is estimated to be around 10,000 yuan. Mr. and Mrs. Kui Bai immediately jumped over the wall and escaped after hearing the alarm. Mrs. Kui Bai fell to the ground due to a misstep and dislocated her joints, which was captured by the robbers. She was beaten and injured, and her head was cut several times, bleeding for up to thirty hours before stopping. Her illness is very serious. It is heard that those who participated in the robbery this time all had local accents. It is said that the bandits originally planned to loot the entire Hengmian, but because they did not have enough people, they first used Hua's house as an experiment.

Wuxi

Robbery in the Eighth District Leads to Murder

Lu Songting, a Taoist priest in Jinjia Lane, Huai Xia Shi Bridge Lane, No. 52 Tu, Eighth District, was 52 years old. His wife, Zhou, was 53 years old. The family had seven or eight mu of fertile land and four children. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 p.m. the night before last, more than 20 robbers suddenly came, all speaking the local dialect, holding flashlights and wooden sticks, and setting off firecrackers to demonstrate their power. They first robbed Lu Pei'guan's house next door, but did not get what they wanted, so they broke into Lu Songting's house and searched at will, and beat Lu Yu and Jin Bao, forcing them to tell where the silver was hidden. At that time, Lu Zhou woke up from her dream and knew that something was wrong, so she escaped from the back door. Unexpectedly, she was spotted by the robbers, and two robbers tracked her down. Zhou was panic-stricken and accidentally fell into the river. The remaining robbers searched Lu's house for about two hours before fleeing with the stolen goods. The total loss was more than 200 yuan. Afterwards, Lu Songting went out to look for his wife and found her dead body in the river. He immediately hired workers to pick her up and prepare her coffin. It has not yet been reported to the county.

Jiangsu Education Institute Holds Agricultural Products Exhibition

The Northern Jiangsu Experimental Area of Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute recently holds an agricultural products exhibition once a year to promote agriculture and arouse farmers' interest in improving agricultural affairs. This year's session is scheduled to be held at the Li Feng headquarters starting on New Year's Day next year. The exhibition will last for two days and will be divided into two categories: ordinary exhibits and testimonial exhibits. The former is agricultural products participated by farmers, and the latter is excellent results from various agricultural organizations, such as the products of various departments and farms of the Education Institute, etc., for demonstration purposes. Currently, the collection of exhibits, as of yesterday, is about 1,600 pieces, including poultry, domestic livestock, melons, fruits, vegetables, rice, and wheat. The district is also preparing to select the best and give awards to encourage farmers to improve. It has hired agricultural experts from the institute, such as Guo Yiquan, to come to the meeting for evaluation. In addition to individual awards, there is also a group award, with townships as the unit. The distribution method is based on the number of products and the number of awards, each accounting for 50%.

Changshu

Private Red Pill Factory Discovered

The County Public Security Bureau received a secret report on the afternoon of the 26th, saying that the Shen family living on Wenchang Street was privately manufacturing red pills, opium, etc., and attached a map. After receiving the report, Director Yin of the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched Inspector Zha Ning of the Bureau, together with the inspectors of the 41st and 2nd Sub-Bureaus, and led the police to the location. According to the map drawn by the reporter, they found a secret factory. There were traps set up in the walls and corners of the house. They immediately seized more than 40 taels of opium, 60 red pills, and some raw materials for making red pills. The owner, Shen Zhifang, and Jiang Zhou, were arrested and taken to the Bureau for investigation.

Yesterday (25th), County Magistrate Ma of Jiangdu informed the original submitter of the situation of inconvenience to comply and asked them to comply.

Party and Government Ban Performances in the Name of Charity

Every winter, many kind-hearted people in Yangzhou have many different charity projects. Last year, someone initiated fundraising by performing plays to help the poor, but as a result, very few poor people benefited. It is heard that someone is initiating fundraising by performing plays again, with the titles of social celebrities listed. Letters were sent to salt merchants and wealthy people to sell play tickets, and the Public Security Direct Sub-Bureau sent police to coerce hotels, singers, and other places to recognize and sell the tickets. This has caused a lot of complaints from the outside world. It is now heard that the party and government organs will strictly ban the fundraising method of performing plays in the name of charity in accordance with the provincial order.

This Year's Xiang An River Transportation Ends

Xiang An has always been a salt delivery point for Huainan, with 120 tickets stipulated for river transportation each year to supplement the insufficiency of sailing transportation. Since Commissioner Miao advocated river transportation last year, the number of river transportation tickets for the An River has been gradually increased year by year. It is estimated that of the 168 tickets to be handled this year, about 140 tickets are allocated to Jinan. They have all been transported by the end of last month, starting from the eighth month. It is heard that the color of the salt inspected in Xiang is white and clean, and the quality is also dry, which is quite welcome by Xiang. Most of the area is made up of old piles accumulated over the years, and recently, the salt production work has been further improved, striving for excellence.

Gaoyou

Western Corps Camp Repeatedly Injured People

Li Hengfeng in Xituan Camp, Sixth District of the county, is a well-off family and has long been coveted by bandits. Unexpectedly, seven or eight robbers with guns suddenly came last night. The family woke up from their dreams and could not escape. Hengfeng was tied by bandits and hung on the beam, and burned under his armpits with fire to force him to tell where the silver was hidden. Hengfeng could not bear the pain and pointed out where the silver was hidden. The bandits saw that their goal had been achieved, so they searched extensively and looted 190 yuan in cash, as well as clothing and sundries. The loss was quite large. They then went to six neighboring houses and looted them all. Later, the army and police stationed in Nan Gan Tuo learned of this and immediately fired shots to chase after them. The bandits fled away. It is heard that Hengfeng was seriously injured and may be in danger of his life.

Jiashan

District Farmers' Association Opposes Rent Payment Standard

The county government convened all the county's organizations and groups to discuss and determine the early and late rice rent payment standards. However, the County Farmers' Association and its affiliated district farmers' associations successively filed petitions, stating that the rent payment standards set by the county government and others violated the principle of 25% rent reduction, increased the burden on tenant farmers, and requested the cancellation of the rent payment standards agreed this time. The board rent must be reduced by 25% according to the amount, and the flower rent must be converted at 37.5%. The County Farmers' Association has submitted an application to the provincial government and has obtained permission from the provincial party headquarters, ordering the county party headquarters to investigate and handle it. At the same time, the Xiaoshan County Party Headquarters also has a request to ban landlords from collecting rent by citing the false rent amount on the lease, and the actual rent amount before the 16th year must be followed to comply with the original meaning of the 25% rent reduction. The County Party Headquarters of this county has issued a notice to all tenants in the county to comply with this dispute.

Mingguang

Ding and Yao Camps Looted by Bandits

Ding and Yao Camps in Puzigang Bao were looted by bandits at dawn yesterday (23rd), and more than 80 people were tied up and nine fast guns were looted. Later, the Mingguang Security Team pursued and rescued 34 hostages. The bandits fled to the Mengjiatai area.

Hefei

County Government Mediates Dispute in Slaughterhouse Industry

Since the Hefei City Butchers' Association implemented public slaughter and distributed the meat to each butcher for sale, each yuan is stipulated to be five jin, and no more is allowed. However, in the rural slaughter industry, each yuan sells six or seven jin. As a result, the city's meat industry sends people to the countryside every day to buy meat and bring it into the city. The city's butchers are afraid that if this trend continues, they will have no business to do, so they send people to wait at each city gate. If they see meat entering the city, they will detain it, causing a great outcry from the meat industry, who unanimously resisted, saying that they would absolutely not be restricted from spending money to buy things. They filed a complaint with the court. Although there were two court hearings, there was still no thorough solution. The meat industry scattered leaflets on the 20th and decided to suspend business to resist to the death. County Magistrate Guo specially ordered four compromise measures to expand the trend: (1) All slaughtered pigs and sheep, whether they have been registered and licensed, or have a tax stamp affixed to the meat, are allowed to be freely bought and sold within the county, regardless of urban or rural areas. (2) The slaughter tax certificate should be kept by the slaughterer. (3) This government will formulate a tax stamp style and order each tax collector to make and distribute it to each market, and all will be stamped with purple on the inside. (4) Residents who buy three jin or less are exempt from inspection, and those who buy more than three jin must have a tax stamp on the meat.

Prison Officer Promoted to Prison Warden

Kong Xianglin, a prison officer in the County Prison, received an order from the High Court yesterday, transferred by the Ministry, approving the resignation of Chen Zhen, the warden of the Third Branch Prison in Suzhou, and appointed the officer to fill the vacancy. Kong's vacant position as a prison officer in this county will be filled by Xing Yuantang, a prison officer who will be transferred from Xixi. After receiving the order, Mr. Kong has prepared to hand over the work and go to Suzhou to take up his new position.

Ticket Prices Have Doubled Compared to Normal

According to the Da Bai News Agency, sources in the transportation industry report that Fuzhou, Zhangzhou, and other places in Fujian Province have recently been subjected to reconnaissance by central government aircraft, causing market chaos and widespread panic. In recent days, relatively wealthy residents of Fuzhou have been moving to Hong Kong and Shanghai. The Fujian pseudo-authorities originally had extremely strict restrictions on incoming and outgoing passengers, but recently, due to the tense situation, they have no time to attend to it. Residents' evacuation seems to be more convenient than before. Therefore, foreign shipping lines operating between Fujian and Hong Kong, and Fujian and Shanghai, have been overcrowded with passengers on every trip, causing the shipping lines to take advantage of the situation and raise ticket prices. Ordinary cabin tickets and large cabin tickets from Fujian to Shanghai have doubled or more, so each shipping line is profiting tenfold.

Collision of the Wanshang and the Lü'an Leads to a Tragic Incident: An Arbitration Tribunal is Organized

Number of Deaths Said to Be Over One Hundred

Letter Invites China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Send Personnel

The matter of the Wanshang Steamer of the Sanbei Company colliding with the Lü'an Steamer in Qizhou, drowning a large number of recruits, has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Because this case is important, Wanshang claims that Lü'an was at fault, but the Lü'an crew denies it. In order to determine which is right and wrong, it has been decided to proceed with arbitration. Further follow-up details will be recorded separately below.

Hankou Navigation Bureau Handles the Aftermath: According to subsequent investigations, the number of newly recruited soldiers who drowned on the spot in the collision of the Wanshang Steamer and the Lü'an soldier transport Steamer was not only more than sixty, and the total number of newly recruited soldiers killed is said to be over one hundred, so the state of the tragic incident is of greater magnitude. After Wanshang arrived in Hankou, Sanbei assumed full responsibility for the entire case after investigating the facts, so the ship continued to operate as usual, and the case was transferred to the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau for handling, in order to demonstrate fairness.

Interrogation of Pilots of Both Ships: Regarding the issue of responsibility for the collision, according to Weng Jiqing, the acting captain of Wanshang, when meeting Lü'an, they blew one horn, and Lü'an also blew one horn. When Wanshang stopped to give way, Lü'an suddenly blew two horns, causing panic and leading to the disaster. It seems that the responsibility lies with the pilot of Lü'an. Later, it was reported that the pilot of Lü'an had fled. Now, the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau has formally notified both parties, ordering Weng Jiqing, the acting captain of Sanbei's Wanshang, and the two pilots on duty at the time, and also summoning Pan Yixiang, the pilot of Lü'an, to appear in court to prepare for a confrontation to clarify the truth.

Organization of a Tribunal for the Tragic Incident: Regarding the tragic incident of the collision of Lü'an, because the matter is serious and the number of deaths is too high, military and political authorities advocate strict investigation of those responsible. In order to handle this case carefully and ensure the accuracy of the facts, the Dian Navigation Administration Bureau has specially organized a tribunal for the tragic incident of the sinking of the Lü'an, dispatching personnel from the Navigation Administration Bureau to conduct on-site investigations and employing impartial navigators to take on the arbitration task.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Designates a Committee Member: The arbitration committee members have been drafted by the Navigation Administration Bureau, and Sanbei and Lü'an have each hired one person to serve as an impartial person for this case. Sanbei Company initially planned to send Zheng Dingxi, owner of the Changxing Ship, as an impartial member. However, due to company relations, he recused himself according to regulations. Yu Qiaqing sent a letter to Liu Hongsheng of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, requesting that Wang Youshi, owner of the Jianguo Steamer, be appointed as an arbitrator. Once the Lü'an side is hired, the court will be immediately opened to conduct investigations and interrogations to arbitrate the responsibility for this tragic incident. Whichever party is proven to be at fault will bear full responsibility for the solution.

Jin Xi's Family Representatives Refute Replies from French and Japanese Consulates

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, Chen Yang and Li Shichang, representatives of Jin Xi's family, have been contacting Korean expatriates in various places and joining forces to protest since Jin Xi was arrested. Recently, Chen and lawyers Lou and Xu went to the Municipal Government again. They were shocked to hear the official replies from the French and Japanese consulates and immediately argued based on reason. According to Chen, the French consulate replied to the Municipal Government, saying that Jin Xi admitted to being Korean in the French Concession police station and that they did not know he had been naturalized as Chinese at the time, so they directly handed him over to the Japanese consulate for detention. From this point of view, the French consulate clearly knew that if Jin Xi had been naturalized as Chinese, they should not have colluded with the Japanese consulate in an illegal arrest. Therefore, setting aside the legal aspect for the time being, it is only necessary to prove that Jin Xi had indeed been naturalized as Chinese, and that the French consulate knew about it beforehand. Furthermore, considering that Jin Xi accompanied his father in naturalizing as Chinese, the original purpose was for the protection of Chinese politics. Moreover, at the time of the illegal arrest by the Japanese consulate, why would he admit to being Korean and give the Japanese consulate an excuse? From a human perspective, even a fool would not do this. Furthermore, there are no records in the police station, so how can they rely on empty words? Moreover, Jin and his father suffered a tragedy last November, and the entire process was covered extensively in Chinese and foreign newspapers. Even Chinese and French agencies have files to consult. In addition, Jin Xi lived on Malang Road in the French Concession for five or six years. How can the French consulate claim that they did not know he had been naturalized as Chinese beforehand? These facts based on reason and evidence are sufficient to prove that the French consulate has a responsibility to demand his return and cannot arbitrarily shirk its responsibility. As for the Japanese consulate's reply to the Municipal Government, stating that Japan has not recognized Jin Xi's transfer to Chinese citizenship and that Jin Xi is not the eldest son of Jin Yongduo, etc., these are even more far-fetched and unreasonable arguments. It is important to know that Jin Xi was naturalized as Chinese along with his father Jin Yongduo. If his father's naturalization as Chinese has been recognized by Japan, then there is no question about Jin Xi's naturalization as Chinese citizenship. It is recalled that last November, when Jin and his father were illegally arrested, the Chinese and French authorities lodged a serious protest based on their naturalized citizenship, and Jin Yongduo was subsequently sent back by the Japanese consulate. This is sufficient to prove that the Japanese consulate had long recognized that Jin and his father had been naturalized as Chinese. Why are they now denying it so strongly? Furthermore, the point that Jin Xi is not the eldest son of Jin Yongduo is even less worthy of mention. Whether he is a nephew or an adopted son, free admission is permitted under Chinese law. As long as there is a naturalization permit, Jin Xi is the eldest son of Jin Yongduo, and there is no doubt that he is a Chinese citizen. Moreover, Japan recognizes Koreans transferring to Chinese citizenship. How can they despise China and uniquely deny it? Some say that the reason why Jin and his father were sent back last year was that the Japanese consul overstepped the French Concession's police power and exchanged them. This is illogical and not worth a smile. In short, based on public reason, the final victory in this case will ultimately belong to us. Civilized countries will definitely express sympathy and assistance and make a judgment based on right and wrong. It is said that weak countries have no diplomacy, which is a nationwide concern. However, if we do not fight for this, international powers will look down on us as a dying nation, and the future of diplomacy will be even more difficult to imagine. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will pay attention to it.

The Executive Yuan Issues an Order Stipulating Commemoration Methods for New Year's Day

No Need for Excessive Extravagance During National Crisis

Still Celebrate as Usual with Holidays and Flag Hanging

The methods for commemorating the 23rd year of the Republic of China on New Year's Day have been ordered by the Executive Yuan for compliance. All agencies will cease operations, and factories will cease work to celebrate. The details are recorded as follows:

Executive Yuan Order: The Executive Yuan orders that:

According to the order of the National Government, the Central Government has decided on the methods for commemorating the 23rd year of the Republic of China on New Year's Day. On this day, all circles across the country will hang flags to celebrate. Party, government, military, and various other agencies, groups, and schools in various places will hold celebrations separately. However, during this national crisis, there is no need for excessive extravagance. In accordance with previous practice, there will still be a three-day holiday from New Year's Day to celebrate. In addition to separate dispatches, this telegraphic order is urgently issued for compliance and to instruct subordinates to comply.

Celebrations in All Circles: On New Year's Day next year, all agencies will uniformly cease operations for three days as usual, schools will have holidays, and factories will cease work for one day in accordance with the Factory Law, with wages paid as usual. Factories with existing customs will still follow the usual practice. All shops and companies will be closed for the holidays. All circles will hang flags to celebrate. The Municipal Government will hold an opening ceremony for the relocation to the new building in the central urban area on New Year's Day. Groups such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce recognize next year as the Women's National Products Year New Year's Day and will hold a car parade and social gathering.

Agency on Duty: During this period of national crisis, all agencies affiliated with the Municipal Government will send personnel to rotate on duty. The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have stipulated three measures: (1) During the holidays before and after this New Year, senior officials should be instructed by the relevant offices, depending on the importance of the affairs they manage, to take turns on duty. The personnel on duty this time will be able to take turns resting later. The number of days of rotation on duty will not be counted as leave, and a list of rotational personnel must be opened and submitted to the Bureau for record. (Work in each section that does not have a significant impact on maintaining traffic does not need to be rotated. The rotational personnel should be limited to those who can take care of things when they happen); (2) Important senior officials should not leave Shanghai rashly during the holidays before and after this New Year unless absolutely necessary; (3) Important senior officials who are not on duty should notify this office of their whereabouts and telephone number at any time for registration, so that they can be contacted in case of emergency.

Various Parties Urge China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Open the Beijing-Hankou Express Passenger Service Early

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's plan to open the Beijing-Hankou express passenger service was proposed last year. Subsequently, the Hubei Construction Department and the Navigation Administration Bureau put forward specific methods. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has accepted the proposal, and the Shipping Department is planning everything. This matter has been reported in this newspaper before. Now, the Hubei Construction Department has negotiated with various railway bureaus, and they have all expressed their sympathy and cooperation, urging the early opening of the service. This matter is of great importance to the Yangtze River traffic, and the details will be recorded further below.

Twenty-Two Hour Voyage: The Beijing-Hankou express passenger service stipulates that it will only stop at Jiujiang port. From Hankou to Beijing, the downstream voyage will only take twenty-two hours. Reaching the capital from Hankou will shorten the voyage to less than a day. The speed is unparalleled. Once it opens, it will definitely be welcomed by passengers, and passengers who usually take foreign shipping line steamers will definitely switch to this express passenger service. Therefore, business development can be assured. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company originally planned to use the Emei Steamer for the first trial voyage, but unfortunately, the ship suddenly hit a reef in Huatanzi, resulting in no ship being dispatched for the time being.

Railway Bureau Has Expressed Sympathy: In order to realize this Yangtze River express passenger service as soon as possible, the Hubei Construction Department has contacted the Hunan-Hubei Railway, the Beijing-Hankou Railway, and the Nanwan Railway separately to handle the connection and transshipment of passengers by land and water between the railways and the express river steamer, and to issue joint train and boat tickets, etc. All the railways believe that this is a measure to develop traffic and facilitate passengers, and they have unanimously agreed and promised to provide assistance. The Hubei Construction Department has also sent a letter to China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, requesting the prompt opening of the service.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway Agrees to Assist: The start and end of the Yangtze River express passenger service are most closely connected to the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, and the relationship is also the greatest. The Beijing-Shanghai Railway authorities have replied to China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Ministry of Communications, stating that the Railway Bureau will do its best to support the opening of the express passenger service in order to achieve cooperation. Special conveniences can also be provided for land and water travel connections.

Minister Zhu's Urging: Minister of Communications Zhu Jiajuahai, upon receiving letters and telegrams from all parties urging the early opening of the Yangtze River express passenger service, has instructed Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, to plan and open the river steamer as soon as possible in order to meet the expectations of all parties and gradually recover the navigation rights that have been lost on the Yangtze River. After receiving the letter from Minister Zhu, Liu has handed it over to the Shipping Department and the Business Department to jointly prepare and find a way to dispatch river steamers in order to open the service for operation as soon as possible.

China National Aviation Corporation Opens Southwest Route, Test Flight Today

Huang Baoxian, Nie Kaiyi, and Others Depart for Hankou Yesterday

From Hankou to Chongqing, Passing Through Hunan, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Yunnan

If Successful, Border Regions Will No Longer Be Isolated

China National Aviation Corporation, after completing the three major trunk lines of Shanghai-Beiping, Shanghai-Chongqing, and Shanghai-Guangdong, is planning to open a southwest route from Hankou, passing through Changsha (Hunan), Guangzhou, Longzhou (Guangxi), Kunming, and reaching Chongqing. A test flight is scheduled for today, departing from Hankou. Details are as follows:

Departed for Hankou Yesterday At 9:30 AM yesterday, the aircraft for the southwest route test flight departed from Longhua Airport, piloted by the company's chief pilot, Anlixun. Accompanying him were Wang Baoxian, director of the business department, and Nie Kaiyi, Chinese director of the aviation department. They arrived safely in Hankou at 4:00 PM.

Flying to Guangzhou This Morning The aircraft is scheduled to take off from Hankou this morning, passing through Changsha in Hunan and reaching Guangzhou for an overnight stay. If the weather is good, it will depart tomorrow for Longzhou in Guangxi, with a short stop planned, and then continue west to Kunming in Yunnan, before flying north from Kunming to Chongqing.

Southwest Transportation After the test flight returns, preparations for the official opening of the route will be made based on the situation. The southwestern provinces, such as Guangxi, Yunnan, and Guizhou, have mountainous terrain and inconvenient transportation. Travel and mail often take more than a month to arrive. Kunming, Longzhou, and other places even find it easier to take a detour through French Indochina. The inconvenience is evident. If this route is successful, the southwestern border regions will no longer be isolated from the Central Plains.

Municipal Federation Sends Telegram Requesting Collection of Stamp Tax from Foreign Nationals

Stamp Tax is Also a National Tax

Foreign Nationals Cannot Be an Exception

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation believes that foreign merchants in Shanghai have not been complying with the commercial treaty by affixing stamp tax. They urgently request that the central authorities promptly collect the tax to uphold the dignity of central laws and regulations. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, requesting the collection of stamp tax from foreign nationals. The original text is as follows: (Titles omitted) "The stamp tax is a central tax, the same as customs and salt taxes, and is not local in nature. In the past, warlords in the Shanghai Special District repeatedly tried to implement the stamp tax, but only required Chinese people to affix it, which was opposed by various business associations and failed. After our National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the association was the first to support and assist in its promotion. All of this is on record. We deeply believe that foreign nationals should be no exception to the national stamp tax, which is the same as customs and salt taxes. Unexpectedly, inspections are now meticulous, and the severe penalties for failing to affix stamps can lead to bankruptcy for merchants, which is not only harmful to the country and the people but also puts the cart before the horse. The provisions of the commercial treaty have become mere formalities, and the dignity of central laws and regulations is lost. Therefore, we specially send this telegram requesting that you promptly remedy the situation, hoping that everyone will share the burden equally and that both persuasion and punishment will be used. In maintaining tax revenue, we will not lose sight of the difficulties faced by merchants. We specially send this telegram for your consideration and implementation. Central tax revenue relies on it." Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation.
