Fan Xudong Plans to Establish Ammonium Sulfate Plant

Banking Sector Has Agreed to Loan

The Authorities Also Commend and Assist

Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, recognizing that ammonium sulfate is not only a large-scale agricultural fertilizer but also has great uses in national defense, but is entirely purchased from abroad at a great cost each year, decided two years ago to establish an ammonium sulfate plant and sent experts to the UK and Germany to negotiate joint ventures. However, due to the other party's harsh conditions, it was not achieved. Local industrialist Fan Xudong, aware of this and with the support of Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, and banking magnate Zhang Gongquan, has decided to raise 7 million yuan to establish an ammonium sulfate plant in Shanghai. All preparations are in place, and it will be opened as soon as the plant site issue is resolved. According to a Central News Agency reporter, the details are as follows:

Annual Demand Ammonium sulfate is the most suitable and best fertilizer for agriculture. According to recent surveys, China's annual demand for ammonium sulfate reaches 150,000 tons. Because there is no domestic production, all of it is imported from abroad, costing about 30 million yuan per year. It is estimated that after the expansion of farmland in the future, the demand will reach more than 5 million tons. (Japan's farmland is less than one-tenth of China's, but its annual demand for ammonium sulfate reaches more than 600,000 tons.) There is indeed a need to establish a plant for domestic production.

Support from All Parties After the plan for a joint venture between the Ministry of Industry and the UK and Germany was announced to be halted, local industrial expert Fan Xudong began to prepare separately. Fan is the manager of Yongli Alkali Company and has spent more than ten years specializing in the research of pure alkali production methods, which has now been completed. Therefore, the company's annual production of pure alkali can supply 70% of the national consumption, which is currently the best achievement in industry. Fan, lacking capital, made various plans. After several months of running around, he has now obtained the support of Zhang Gongquan, Bei Songsheng, Li Fusun, Chen Guangfu, Xu Xinliu, Zhou Zuomin, and other powerful figures in the local banking sector, who have agreed to loan Fan 7 million yuan under certain conditions as capital for establishing the ammonium sulfate plant. Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, and Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo have also praised his ambition and promised to do their best to assist.

Progress of the Plan Since obtaining the support of all parties, Fan's progress has been very smooth. All internal preparations have been largely resolved, and he is currently working on the plant site issue. It will be opened as soon as the plant site issue is resolved. The location of the plant site has been decided to be in Shanghai. As for the machinery, it is said that negotiations are underway for ordering.

Ministry of Communications Orders Shanghai Telegraph Bureau to Find Ways to Use Wheatstone Receiving Machines

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau received instructions from the Ministry of Communications yesterday, stating, "After investigating the interference caused by electrified lines, significant work is needed to avoid it. According to the report from the Tianjin Bureau's business director, 'When interference occurs on the lines, the symbols received by the Wheatstone receiving machine are clearer than those received by the undulator receiving machine. Tianjin-Qingdao and Tianjin-Jinan direct lines have successively switched to using Wheatstone receiving machines.' Your bureaus should immediately follow the example of the Tianjin Bureau and find ways to switch to using Wheatstone receiving machines to avoid interference and install surge arresters to increase the speed. Also, the resistance of the coils of the Wheatstone receiving machines in your bureaus when connected in series and parallel, and the sending and receiving current of each express line, should be thoroughly investigated and reported. Furthermore, the Wheatstone receiving machine requires a larger working current. If the receiving current in your bureaus is too weak, making it difficult to work, you can add a standard relay to ensure smooth communication. Please comply with these instructions and report accordingly."

Hydrographic Office Announces Lightship Off-Station Signals

From Dawn on January 1st

Shipping Community Should Pay Special Attention

The Hydrographic Office of the Navy Department has issued an announcement regarding the "off-station" signals of lightships along the coast of the Republic of China and the Yangtze River, so that the shipping community should pay special attention. The original text states, "From dawn on January 1, 1934, all manned lightships currently managed by the Maritime Customs Service will display the following signals when they leave their original positions: Article 1: If a lightship drifts away from its original position due to dragging anchor or breaking of the mooring chain, its beacon and fog signal will be stopped immediately. Article 2: If possible, its topmark will also be removed immediately. Article 3: When a lightship is navigating, its signals should be the same as those used by ordinary ships. If the lightship is using its own engine power, the signals displayed during the day should be applied according to the first item or second item of Article 4. Article 4: When a lightship drifts from its original position due to dragging anchor or breaking of the mooring chain, it should display the following special signals: (Item 1) Lightships above Yaogang Mouth in the Yangtze River: (A) Two red flags are displayed at the end of the mast's spar during the day, and the international communication flag P.C. (This ship is not in its original position) is displayed at the other end. (B) At night, if the lightship originally displays a white light, it should change to displaying a red light at the bow and stern of the ship. If it originally displays a red light or a red and white light, it should display a white light at the bow and stern of the ship. (Item 2) Lightships along the coast: (A) A large black spherical marker is hung at the front and rear during the day. (B) A red light is hung at the front and rear at night. If, for any reason, the aforementioned daytime signals cannot be used, or the lightship's original marker is the same as this signal, a red flag should be used to replace the black spherical marker. The following prescribed signals should be used as a supplement to the preceding signals: (C) The international communication flag P.C. (This ship is not in its original position) is additionally displayed during the day. (D) At least every fifteen minutes, a red and white flare signal should be fired simultaneously. If, for any reason, the flare signal cannot be used, a red and white light should be lit simultaneously instead."

Great China Workers Resumed Work in Compliance with Orders, Factory Refused, Conflict Occurred

Seven Workers Arrested and Released Immediately

The Labor Side Petitioned This Morning, Requesting Thorough Investigation

The Great China Rubber Factory on Xujiahui Road employs more than 1,600 workers and has a prosperous business. The factory workers recently initiated the organization of a trade union, which was envied by the factory, which used the excuse to dismiss the union organizers. The Municipal Party Committee approved the resumption of work, but the factory refused, causing a conflict. Details are as follows:

Course of the Dispute Guo Junchen, Tao Shiying, and nine other workers of the Great China Rubber Factory were dismissed by the factory under the pretext of non-compliance with the insurance policy procedures because they initiated the preparation of a trade union. The labor side submitted a petition to the party and government agencies, requesting assistance. After investigation by the Municipal Party Committee, it was considered that the factory's dismissal of the workers was not justified. The Municipal Party Committee immediately approved both labor and management, limiting the workers to complete the guarantee procedures within ten days and return to work.

Refusal to Resume Work After receiving the approval from the Municipal Party Committee, the workers immediately prepared the guarantee procedures and went to the factory at 8:00 AM yesterday with the approval from the Party Committee to resume work. The factory initially refused to meet with them. It was not until 1:00 PM that the engineer Ye Zhiyun replied to the workers, saying that the factory refused the workers to resume work. The workers handed over the approval from the Party Committee for review, but it was torn up by Yang Bingjun, an employee of the factory, who immediately closed the factory door tightly, causing a reaction from the workers and a major conflict.

Conflict Occurred The workers believed that the factory had torn up the approval from the Party Committee and closed the factory door tightly, showing contempt for the superior and intentionally oppressing them. Therefore, the crowd was angry and a conflict occurred. One of the factory employees had his clothes torn, and both sides suffered minor injuries. The factory, seeing the serious situation, immediately called the Wenlin Road Police Station, falsely claiming robbery. After receiving the report, the police station sent two police cars and more than 20 police officers to suppress the situation, stationing police around the factory gate and entering to arrest seven workers, including Guo Junchen and Tao Shiying, and took them to the Wenlin Road Police Station for interrogation. As a result, it was considered that the matter was a labor-management dispute and not a robbery. The case was declared inadmissible, and the seven arrested were immediately released.

Petition This Morning The labor side believes that the factory violated the orders of the superior, tore up the instructions, and falsely reported a robbery, which is illegal. In addition to hiring a lawyer to file a lawsuit according to law, they also decided to petition the party and government agencies this morning, requesting a thorough investigation and handling.

Municipal Ferry Opens New Route

Youlong Pier to Tongren Pier

The municipal ferry service in this city has been striving to expand in recent years. The cross-river ferry currently operates routes including: (1) Dongchang Road to Dongmen Road, (2) Qichangzhan to Weissigong Pier, (3) Qingning Temple to Dinghai Bridge, etc. There are about 20,000 passengers per day. All ferries are made of steel hulls, safe and comfortable, fast and unobstructed by wind. The citizens find it convenient. Now it is learned that the Municipal Ferry Management Office, in order to expand the routes and increase the convenience of the citizens, has decided to open a new cross-river route between Youlong Pier in Pudong and Tongren Pier on the Bund of Nanjing Road in Puxi. All construction work on Youlong Pier and the ferries has been completed, and services will start on the 28th of this month, operating daily from 5:00 AM to 8:00 PM, running back and forth every twenty minutes. From 5:00 AM to 7:00 AM in the morning and evening, the fare is uniformly 5 copper coins per passenger, and at other times, it is uniformly 8 copper coins per passenger. Tickets are purchased in advance at the pier and then boarded the ship. All methods of carrying goods are the same as those of other cross-river routes.

Funeral This Afternoon

Mr. Yao Zirang, a senior gentleman, is respected for his knowledge and morality, and his disciples are all over the world. They are all scholars. He is upright and strong, and he is the only mouthpiece for the people. All circles rely on him as the Great Wall. He devoted himself to the country and local affairs in the capacity of civilian leading people. Having given six decades to those efforts, he unfortunately passed away at 9:10 PM on the 26th (two days ago) due to old age and without illness. All circles were deeply saddened by the news. His family scheduled the funeral for him on the afternoon of the 28th. Mr. Yao was brilliant when he was young during the Qing Dynasty Xianfeng Year, and he entered the school at the age of fifteen. Guangxu Yiyou Juren. He studied history, politics and law

Portrait of Mr. Yao Zirang

Economics and arithmetic at Longmen Academy in his early years. From then on almost twenty years. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, the improvement of municipal education in various parts of our country all took Shanghai as an example. And the actions in our Shanghai to promote benefits and eliminate malpractices, such as abolishing academies, establishing schools, demolishing city walls, building roads, as well as establishing water and electricity, handling security, organizing land, and repairing records, etc., were all planned and managed by Mr. Yao and solidified. Mr. Yao served as the Director of the Education Promotion Institute, Dean of Nanyang Public School, Director of the Engineering Bureau, Shanghai City Economic Director, Chairman of the Defense Regiment, Director of the Real Estate Office, Director of the Land Survey Bureau, Director of the Charity Association, Member of the House of Representatives of the National Assembly, and opposed Cao Kun's bribery election rate and returned with the Jiangsu National Assembly members, Jiangsu Provincial Council Member, and Speaker of the Shanghai Municipal Council. As for Mr. Yao's works, they are scattered in various collections, and his great works include Shanghai County Chronicles, Gongnan Water Conservancy Chronicles, Jiangsu Provincial Chronicles, and Draft Law of Etiquette.

Disaster Victims Are Sleeping Outdoors Without Clothes to Ward off the Cold

Relief Workers in Henan Repeatedly Telegraph Inquiries

The Joint Association for Emergency Relief of the Yellow River Flood in Shanghai, due to the large number of refugees in the disaster areas of Henan Province, and as winter arrives, without clothes to ward off the cold, various philanthropists have donated 7,850 pieces of new cotton clothing, which were shipped in four batches to Hankou from October 27th to December 22nd, and then transported by the Pinghan and Longhai Railways to various parts of Henan for distribution. However, the railway authorities, due to the congestion of goods and insufficient allocation of vehicles, and the Ministry of Finance having approved half-price accounting for charitable organizations transporting relief goods, have delayed transportation, and they have not yet been delivered. The association's relief workers, Ma Zuwu, and Hongsan, deeply saddened by the sight of disaster victims sleeping outdoors without clothes, have repeatedly telegraphed inquiries about the prompt delivery of the cotton clothing to save the disaster victims.

Ministry of Finance Actively Rectifying Currency System

Already Ordered Financial Bureaus in Various Provinces

To Buy and Melt Down Inferior Miscellaneous Coins

In order to unify the national currency system and address the financial impact of inferior coins, the Ministry of Finance has specifically instructed the financial bureaus in various provinces to purchase and melt down the inferior miscellaneous coins circulating on the market in the shortest possible time. The main points of the instructions are summarized as follows: (1) Investigate and ban inferior copper coins in various provinces and cities, and set a deadline for recall or melting, to be handled by the competent authorities in each province. (2) Crack down on private minting of silver dollars in various provinces. (3) Prohibit the use of light-weight copper coins. (4) Investigate and ban the unauthorized issuance of banknotes.

Seamen's Union Concessions from Taikoo after Negotiations over Wusong Ship Case

Seamen Everywhere Indignantly Request Blocking of Ship Passage

Zhengda Comprador Refuses to Register with the Union, Warning Letter Sent

The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union, after overturning the resolution of the Wusong ship dispute by the Guangdong Seamen's Industrial Union, directly negotiated with Taikoo, and the company has made concessions on conditions such as registering workers. Also, the comprador of the Zhengda ship of Datong Company refused to register with the union, and a unified response has been decided upon. Details are provided below:

Taikoo Agrees to Concessions: Since the Guangdong Seamen's Industrial Union resolved the Wusong ship dispute with Taikoo Company, seamen in various places have expressed dissatisfaction with this resolution, and the workers on the Wusong ship themselves have also joined in the denial. The Seamen's Union then took charge of the negotiations, and after repeated delegations by secretaries Hou Dachun and Sun Liping, the company expressed concessions on measures such as reorganizing seamen, and agreed to revisions. The union must wait until the entire resolution is overturned before proposing appropriate conditions, so a resolution should be possible soon.

Seamen Everywhere Indignant: Seamen in various places, deeming the handling of the Guangdong Seamen's Industrial Union inappropriate, have unanimously requested the Seamen's Union to resolve the Wusong incident, expecting it to not yield and not sell out the seamen. They also expressed their intention to effectively blockade Taikoo ships nationwide. The union, wanting to avoid a split during this period, will adopt this method if no results are achieved. According to Standing Committee member Zhang Jianbai, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, the union can cut off the entry and exit of Taikoo ships at all ports nationwide within four days of a split. Guangdong seamen also expressed their approval of the union's actions.

Dealing with Zhengda Comprador: Zhu Zuoting, the comprador of the Tongyang class Zhengda ship of Datong Company, does not allow 150 workers to register with the union. The workers are planning effective countermeasures and are currently brewing a strike. The Shanghai Seamen's Branch has reported this to the union, requesting a cessation. The union is extremely angry at the comprador's illegal obstruction. Since the seamen's registration has been approved and implemented by the central government, it cannot be easily suspended due to the obstruction of one comprador. In addition to offering guidance, two countermeasures have been established: (1) Send a letter to the company for correction and warning. (2) Otherwise, stop the ship from sailing.

According to news from the Naval Headquarters in Shanghai, after drafting the regulations for the management of pilots in various ports of China's rivers and seas, the organization of the management committee has been underway. However, due to various problems, it has not yet been established. The establishment of the Pilot Management Committee is deemed necessary as soon as possible. Regarding the representative to be appointed by the Navy, the Ministry has appointed Xu Jixiang, Director of the Naval Affairs Department, as the representative and has consulted the Ministry of Finance for review.

Kidnapping Bandits Are Active Again, Two Kidnappings in 24 Hours

He Boxian Kidnapped on Xizang Road Yesterday Morning

Huang Jinfu Abducted on Dunxin Road the Night Before

He Boxian: He Boxian, a prominent steel businessman, is 27 years old and lives in Donghua Lane, Xizang Road. Due to his busy schedule, he has a Morris sedan, license number 3496 in the concession and 5997 in the municipal government. Yesterday morning at approximately 11 a.m., He was leaving his house for business and was about to step into the car when four men suddenly jumped out from the lane, each holding a handgun. They seized him, and three bandits got into the back seat with him. One bandit was in the front, monitoring He's driver, Shen Baokang, ordering him to drive the car west on Race Course Road. The driver had no choice but to obey. When they reached the vicinity of New Dagu Road, the bandits ordered the car to stop, pushed the driver Shen Baokang out of the car, and the bandit in the front seat drove off quickly to the west. When the driver was pushed out of the car, the bandits threw a short note beside him, instructing Zhu to hand it over to He's father, He Fangfu. At that time, the driver Zhu Baokang was afraid of endangering his master's life, so he did not dare to speak. After the bandits went far, he rushed back home to deliver the letter and report everything. He's father, upon learning of this, hurriedly discussed with his family. The content of the bandit's letter stated that He had been kidnapped and that they were not allowed to report to the police station. They should wait for contact, and He would be released soon. Afterwards, the Old Gate and New Gate police stations were also notified and immediately dispatched detectives to search for him, but he was nowhere to be found. Therefore, the police station notified all police agencies in the city, requesting assistance. However, as of 10 p.m., the car had not been found.

Huang Jinfu: Huang Jinfu, a native of Dongdi, residing at No. 3, Dong Wangjia Lane, Yidingpan Road, in the Chinese area, is nearly sixty years old. He started from scratch through diligence and thrift and is not wealthy. He has two sons. The eldest son, Jin Di, is 26 years old and works at the Donations Office of the British Public Works Bureau. The second son, Jin Fu, also known as Feng Hao, is 20 years old and works as an accountant at the Xinxing Milk Stand at No. 1040, Zhangjiazhai, Daxilu. He is used to leaving early and returning late. The day before yesterday (the 26th) at 5:15 p.m., Huang was walking home because he was very close to his house. Unexpectedly, two bandits suddenly jumped out from the side of the road, each with a handgun, and warned Huang not to make a sound. They forced him into a car parked in front of No. 107, Dunxin Road, and sped off to the west. By the time patrol officers Zhao Kunhe and Xin Haipu from the Daxilu substation of the Second Division of the Sixth District arrived, the bandits were long gone. They immediately reported to Inspector Qiang Yude to investigate the situation. According to his family, Huang was wearing a black-gray self-made cloth overcoat and black velvet shoes when he was kidnapped. There were no threatening letters beforehand, and no letters from the bandits have been received since the kidnapping. The whole family is very anxious.

Unemployed Youth Devises Clever Plan to Steal Huge Sum of Money

Scaring Away Apprentices by Pretending to be a Ghost

Eventually Fully Exposed

Yikang Money Shop, located at No. 68, Avenue Edward VII, has been in business for decades. Due to the effective management of the Zhenjiang native Huang Zibin, the manager, the business has grown year by year, making it a well-known money shop in the French Concession. Yao Lizheng, a 28-year-old fellow townsman of the manager, Huang, knew Huang well and often visited. He used to work in a rubber factory in Shanghai, but was recently suspended for misconduct. Being unemployed and having no means of support, and because his expenses in Shanghai were high, he stayed at the Yikang Money Shop, hoping to find a job. The partners of the shop treated Yao with respect because he was the manager's friend. The shop received silver dollars every day, which were packed in boxes and piled up in the parlor and upstairs. A cellar was set up in a small room behind the parlor to store banknotes, covered with wooden boards. At night, the apprentices laid their beds on the cellar cover to guard it, and Yao also slept on a bed next to the cellar. Yao saw the partners open the cellar to take out cash during the day and saw that the cellar was full of large stacks of banknotes. Being unemployed and short of money, he was tempted by greed and had the evil idea of stealing the money. However, he could not find a way to start because the apprentices slept on the cellar at night. After much deliberation, he came up with a clever plan. When the top apprentice was asleep, he would gently tap the apprentice's head with something. When the apprentice woke up screaming and chasing, Yao would pretend to be asleep and not know anything. After several nights, the apprentice, being young and inexperienced, thought it was a ghost and was too scared to sleep on the cellar anymore and slept elsewhere. On the night of the 15th of this month, only Yao slept in the original place. Seeing that the opportunity had come, he seized it that night when all the partners were asleep and it was quiet, and he lifted the wooden cover of the cellar and stole several bundles of banknotes, totaling 7,600 yuan, and hid them on his body. The next morning when the market opened, he sneaked out and deposited the money at the house of his mistress, Yu Xiuying, a fellow townsman, at No. 538, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. He still pretended to be calm and returned to the shop. When the partners opened the cellar to withdraw money, they discovered the theft and were greatly shocked. They reported it to the French police station, which sent detectives to investigate. They questioned all the partners and Yao, but Yao denied it and was very eloquent, so there were no clues. Yao was lucky enough to escape. The detective reported back to the police chief and continued to investigate. Yao thought that the matter was over. To avoid further suspicion, he left the shop and opened Room No. 5 at the Beiyang Hotel at the intersection of Beizhejiang Road and Jielu. The detectives suspected Yao the most, so they sent someone to secretly investigate him. Yao thought he could get away with it and took out some of the banknotes to buy new clothes, such as a gray crepe silk new fur robe, and showed off his wealth, not knowing that he was being followed. Everything he did was learned. The informants reported to the French police detectives Lu Zhulin and Zhang Daorong, who led detectives Liu Jinrong and Wu Jiahui to arrest Yao on the afternoon of the day before yesterday and took him to the police station for questioning. Yao knew that the matter had been exposed and could not be concealed, so he confessed everything. He had spent 1,400 yuan on buying things and paying off debts, and the remaining 6,200 yuan was at his mistress's house. The detective took Yao to the Public Security Bureau of the First Branch of the Fifth District of Zhabei and requested the police to go to No. 538, Yongxing Road to arrest Yao's mistress, Yu Xiuying. 6,200 yuan of the original stolen banknotes were found in a suitcase and taken to the station. After questioning by the station chief, Yu and the stolen goods were ordered to be sent to the main bureau for verification. The detectives brought Yao back to the police station and sent him to the Second Special District Court for questioning yesterday. In the afternoon at 3 p.m., Judge Sun Pengxian sat in the eighth criminal court for trial. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi said that the police station had not yet investigated the case, and the defendant's mistress, who had received the stolen goods, was currently detained in the Public Security Bureau. He requested a postponement, temporarily detaining the defendant, and requested the court to prepare a document to transfer his mistress's case to investigate and prosecute. After reviewing the report, the court briefly questioned Yao Lizheng and then announced a postponement to January 5, 23rd year of the Republic of China, for a retrial. The defendant was returned to custody.

The Truth about the Seventh Prize Drawing Method of the Third Aviation Lottery

According to the person in charge of the lottery office yesterday, the seventh prize drawing method published in yesterday's newspaper had too many errors. The method set by this office is to prepare 1,000 small balls (not 500) numbered from 000 to 999 (not 499). If the numbers 7, 8, and 9 are drawn from the above 1,000 small balls, then all numbers with the same last three digits as 7, 8, and 9 will win the seventh prize. Also, the date for the next drawing is set for March 2, not February 28.

A Murder Case Occurred Late at Night Near Zhaofeng Garden

Competing for the Position of Foreman of a Wood Factory, Colleagues Killed Each Other

At approximately 11:20 p.m. the night before yesterday, a shooting murder case suddenly occurred near the Sujiajiao small bridgehead next to the Zhaofeng Garden on Avenue Haig. The details are recorded as follows:

Reason for the Feud: Luo Changfa, a native of Jintan, 30 years old, currently residing at No. 22, Zhongshan Bridge, Husi, served as the foreman of the Jingyi Wood Factory in Zhoujiaqiao, North Beach, on the 16th day of the eighth lunar month of this year. However, the factory's general manager, Qi Yugen, immediately approached Luo and introduced a man from Jiushan, Yuan Yongshi, to cooperate with Luo in the position of foreman. At that time, Luo, under the order of the manager, implemented the cooperation between the two. Since then, the two went to the factory every day to serve, and they felt quite congenial, and there were no conflicts for two months. However, on December 1, after Luo received the work money in the factory, Yuan suddenly led a large number of workers to calculate wages with Luo, deliberately making things difficult for him. They were twisted and sent to the Sixth District Police Station to pay a fine and released. Then Yuan asked Luo to leave his job and let him take the position alone. Luo did not answer, and Yuan did not go to the factory.

Shooting Murder: Three days ago, Yuan had gone to Luo to question him and said that if you were not willing to leave the job, he would use a gun to deal with him. Luo was afraid of misfortune, so he avoided lodging elsewhere. At more than 11 o'clock the night before yesterday, Luo suddenly passed through the youth association lane entrance on Avenue Haig and happened to meet Yuan's younger brother, Yuan Yongtang, who was driven by Yuan to the lane. Not far down the road, he saw Yuan Yongshi and a person named Zhang Shizhi come. Then the three people surrounded Luo and walked. When they arrived at the small bridge, Yuan and Zhang each fired a gun at Luo. Luo was shot and fell to the ground. Yuan and others saw that their goal had been achieved and fled.

Wounded Report: It was late at night, and the place was secluded. After a while, Luo endured the pain and crawled to the entrance of the youth association lane and reported to the No. 2 post police officer of the Sixth District. He was taken back to the district. The district officer found that Luo had been shot twice. One bullet passed through the cotton robe, and one bullet hit his right leg. Blood was flowing. After a brief interrogation, he was sent to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment, avoiding a threat to his life. Police were dispatched to investigate and found two bullet casings.

Arrested Murderer: Yesterday, District Chief Tan sent police and detectives to Zhoujiaqiao to arrest the murderers Yuan Yongshi (33 years old, Shandong native) and Yuan Yongtang (31 years old, Shandong native). Only Zhang Shizhi had fled upon hearing the news. They were taken back to the district. After an interrogation by District Officer Xing, he was sentenced and sent to the Bureau for interrogation.

Chance Encounter Reveals Long-Lost Love

Zhang Bohe Heartlessly Abandons Her, Ignoring Their Past Affection

Fang Aying Can No Longer Tolerate It, Files a Criminal Self-Complaint

Fang Aying, a young woman residing at No. 49, Taian Lane, Tiantong Road, is only twenty-three years old. At the age of fourteen, she was quite developed, so she seemed like an adult, and she understood the ways of the world, so she was seduced by a man named Zhang Bohe and was raped. After her parents learned of this, they questioned Zhang, and Zhang promised to formally marry Aying as his wife when she reached adulthood. In the meantime, he temporarily cohabited with her. Aying's parents, because the matter was already done, did not want to make excessive demands, and the matter was settled. Two years later, Aying gave birth to a son, who is now seven years old. But when Aying was eighteen years old, Zhang, fearing that he would have to fulfill his marriage promise, claimed to be going to Japan for trade and asked Aying to take good care of their son. Before leaving, he gave her three hundred gold coins for household expenses. Aying did not understand this kind of excuse for traveling far away to escape, so she was fooled. From then on, the mother and daughter were lonely and looked forward to her husband's return every day, but they never saw him again. In July of this year, they unexpectedly met on the road. At that time, Aying was filled with joy and sorrow, thinking that the broken mirror could be reunited, but Zhang's attitude was completely different from the past. He regarded Aying as a stranger. Even after Aying repeatedly begged him to take her back, Zhang's heart was like a stone, and he turned and left. Aying was extremely angry at this encounter and became ill after returning home. She has only recently recovered slightly. She hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-complaint against Zhang in the First Special District District Court, saying that Zhang had abandoned her and was guilty of the crime of harming public morals under Article 244 of the Criminal Code and the crime of abandonment under Article 310. In addition to requesting the court to summon him for trial, she also filed a civil lawsuit, saying that the child was already seven years old and the annual support fee was calculated at 300 yuan, so he should pay back 2,100 yuan. Also, because the plaintiff is now twenty-three years old and has a chronic illness, she cannot remarry in the future, so the defendant should bear the maintenance fee of 360 yuan per year until the age of sixty, a total of thirty-seven years, totaling 13,320 yuan. According to the statement, the court issued a summons based on the defendant's address and sent police to summon the defendant to the Yongtaichang Foreign Goods Company across from the Sino-Western Pharmacy on the Fourth Road. At 2 p.m. yesterday, he was to attend the hearing in the Third Court. At that time, the defendant was not seen. According to the court police, there was only Zhang Wubo in the foreign goods company, not Zhang Bohe, so the summons was not accepted. Judge Xiao stated that because the defendant was not summoned to court, the case could not proceed. He then announced a postponement and waited for the defendant to be summoned before the retrial.

Robbery with Gunshot Wound Leading to Death

Name of Robber: Xia Changgen

Lu Caisheng Dies Tragically After Eating Pufferfish

Entire Family Eats, One Person Poisoned

Wife, Children, and Both Sons and Daughters Show No Ill Effects

Lu Caisheng, a 36-year-old boatman from Yuncaobang, Wusong, had a wife, three sons, and two daughters. The day before yesterday afternoon, his wife bought two fresh pufferfish to cook for dinner. He immediately went ashore to buy reeds and green fruits to try to save himself, but the poisoning was too deep. He received ineffective medical treatment and died tragically in the middle of the night. Yesterday, a coffin was prepared for his burial. However, his wife and children, who also ate the fish, showed no ill effects. This is both fortunate and unfortunate.

Incoming

Railway Operations and the Coming Year's Plans for Intermodal Transport (Continued)

(B) Vigorously Implementing Responsible Intermodal Transport of Goods on National Railways: The railways of various parts of the country are like the blood vessels of a person's body. Only when each road is connected to each other, the branches and trunks maintain each other, and the distant and near correspond to each other, can the effect of concerted cooperation and smooth transportation be achieved. If each road governs itself and does not have a connection with each other, it is like the blood vessels in various parts of the human body being unconnected. Even if the local part is complete and healthy, the entire human body will inevitably be unsustainable. This is clear and should be deeply understood. Intermodal transport of railways in our country was started 20 years ago. Due to repeated disasters and lack of talent, the intermodal transport business is still extremely immature. Although passenger transport has been reorganized and improved, it is still far from the realm of perfection. As for the intermodal transport of goods, it has been completely suspended since the Republic of China. Checking the relationship between the intermodal transport of goods and the national economy and people's livelihood is twice as close and twice as important as passenger transport. At a time when the national economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, it has been allowed to reach this point. Although this is due to external resistance, it is also due to the fact that the railway itself has not done its best. Therefore, in the past year or so, while promoting responsible transport on each road, we have also promoted responsible intermodal transport on each road. It cannot be said that the function of transportation is fully fulfilled if there is transportation without responsibility. It cannot be said that the function of transportation is fully fulfilled if there is responsibility without intermodal transport. It must be that each road can be responsible for intermodal transport before it can be said that the function of transportation has been fully fulfilled and the practical benefits for merchants and the people can be achieved. On September 1, 21 years ago, Jinpu, Jinghu, and Huhangyong Roads implemented responsible transportation, and on October 1, they implemented responsible intermodal transport. It is a pity that other roads did not fully join due to various relationships and difficulties, and only agreed to partial intermodal transport. The method is not unified, and freight transport is naturally hindered. In order to break through this difficulty, we gathered colleagues from the Business Department Intermodal Transport Office and the Goods Responsible Transportation Committee of the Ministry to compile the Provisional Measures for Responsible Freight Intermodal Transport on Railways. Based on theory and with reference to the facts, it took several months and dozens of meetings to complete. In September 22, the Ministry convened the 16th National Intermodal Transport Conference, and all intermodal transport measures were separately determined and scheduled to be implemented on November 1. What should be strived for thereafter is strict implementation and maximum promotion, so that 23 years of the Republic of China can be the time for the revival of freight intermodal transport on railways in our country.

(C) Implementing Water and Land Intermodal Transport: Railways are a sharp tool for land transportation, and ships are a sharp tool for water transportation. A country's territory has land and water. Railways should not only be connected to each other, but also be connected to ships. Only then can a country's transportation be called convenient, and the transportation of passengers and goods can be agile. This is a long-standing goal of water and land intermodal transport. The only state-run waterway transport agency in our country with a relatively complete scale is the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. If you want the early realization of water and land intermodal transport, the only way is for state-owned roads to engage in intermodal transport with the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company as soon as possible. Therefore, at the 16th National Intermodal Transport Conference, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was invited to join in the compilation of water and land intermodal transport measures. It was decided that the Intermodal Transport Office of the Ministry would represent state-owned roads and sign an intermodal transport contract with China Merchants Steam Navigation Company based on the established measures. Then, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will negotiate with the relevant roads to negotiate detailed rules for intermodal transport. These contracts and detailed rules have now been negotiated and are ready to be announced and implemented. All passengers and goods in coastal and Yangtze River ports can be intermodal transported with state-owned roads.

(D) Preparing for Railway-Automobile Intermodal Transport: Railways are intermodal transported with each other, and railways are intermodal transported with ships. However, under today's circumstances, it is still not possible to complete the intermodal transport of a country's transportation agencies. In addition to railways and ships, there are also two types of transportation agencies: air transportation and automobile transportation. Air transportation is still in its infancy, and its intermodal transport with railways can be discussed later. However, railway-automobile intermodal transport needs to be actively carried out. The reason is that automobile transportation has been developing rapidly in recent years, with a trend of rapid development. The situation in foreign countries will not be discussed here. In our country, although the construction of highways and the preparation of automobiles by various provinces and individuals are in the midst of national crisis, there is still a vigorous trend. The highways in our country are rarely parallel to the railways, and are mostly extended from a certain station on the railway to a certain place in the interior. These small towns and remote areas are mostly unreachable by railways, and all their transactions and transfers depend on automobiles. If they can be intermodal transported with railways, the agricultural, mining, and forestry products of the interior areas through which the automobile roads pass can be exported by automobiles, and the manufactured products of the cities reached by the railways can be imported by railways. At the same time, due to convenient transportation, the number of passengers between urban and rural areas and the number of trips per person will gradually increase. Then, the railway will be the transfer station for automobiles, and the automobile will be the nutrient line for the railway. Each will benefit from the other and complement each other. It goes without saying that both railways and automobiles will benefit from this, and it will be more helpful to facilitate commerce and tourism, develop industries, develop the national economy, and communicate social culture. Therefore, the preparation of railway-automobile intermodal transport is also a current and urgent task. The outline of railway-automobile intermodal transport was also discussed and decided at the 16th National Intermodal Transport Conference. It is planned that each road will investigate the relevant automobile roads and negotiate intermodal transport measures based on the previous outline to facilitate transportation and benefit merchants and the people. (To be continued)

Chunqiu

Thinking about the Inauguration of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the Civil War

— Sincerity

I feel that "national crisis" is not really something to grieve over, nor something to mourn. If everyone can clearly understand the relationship of the national crisis and their own responsibilities, resolving the national crisis would not be difficult. Perhaps the entire nation could even be invigorated and strengthened by it. The most heartbreaking thing is nothing other than "civil war"!

Regardless of whether the old man's handling was improper or not, I believe that on this dilapidated ship, if everyone insists on causing internal strife, then there will only be one outcome: mutual destruction! We can completely disregard major issues such as international status, world trends, and plunder by powerful neighbors, etc., and just take the small Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway as an example to make everyone clearly aware of the lamentable nature of civil war!

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway was initiated by Mr. Zhang Jingjiang. Over the years, thanks to the Zhejiang Construction Department's arduous efforts, it was built using the most economical methods. This railway, which is 360 kilometers long, has now been fully completed. The convenience it offers to merchants and people in the western Zhejiang area is truly immeasurable. What makes us especially happy are two points: first, the construction engineering of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway was entirely planned by our Chinese experts, and no foreigners were ever consulted; second, although the funding for the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway also came from mortgages, it never borrowed a single penny of foreign debt. Therefore, I feel that even if the transportation function of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is not considered, its planning and construction alone can be said to be a glorious chapter in Chinese construction history. However, unfortunately, just as it was fully completed, and passenger and freight trains could directly travel between the Jiangbian and Yushan areas, the detestable civil war was launched from Fujian, and it happened to be nearby. Let us think about it: such a good construction project, not to mention the material aspect, but only in terms of the spiritual aspect, if it is truly damaged or halted due to military affairs, wouldn't that be like a very good painting, just completed by an artist with much effort, suddenly being torn to shreds by someone, spoiling the beautiful scenery?

I love my motherland and only hope that it can have a day of revival. Every time I see a new construction, my heart always has indescribable joy. However, even if there is new construction but it is immediately destroyed, it is even more heartbreaking than not having construction at all.

Friends, is there a way to stop the civil war? I pray for your great invention!

Nanjing Songstress Praised by French Novelist

— Chun Liu

French novelist de Gopeira traveled from Nanjing to Beiping and suddenly gave a "woman theory" to newspaper reporters, saying that Chinese women were indescribably beautiful, and Suzhou women were especially beautiful. He cited as evidence: "I heard Chinese songs in the Confucius Temple in Nanjing. There was a Suzhou songstress named Xue Yanqin. Her graceful demeanor on stage captivated my soul for several days," and so on. As a result, he was protested by Beiping female writer Pan Junying, who criticized de Gopeira as an uncultured person, saying that he looked down on Chinese women.

Regarding this case, we will not discuss how de Gopeira will answer. However, we in Nanjing know for sure that there is no Xue Yanqin among the songstresses in the Confucius Temple. We only know that there is a Xue Youqin who sings Qingyi roles at the Star Theatre, and she is not called Xue Yanqin (the old star Yanqin has already married in Beiping). In de Gopeira's original remarks, he mentioned something about graceful demeanor on stage, which proves that he was definitely not referring to the women in the "flower tea houses" of the Confucius Temple, but rather the Kunling Xue Youqin in the old-style theaters.

But who is Xue Youqin? It is said that she is Rong Lijuan's fellow apprentice, Rong Sujuan, both from Mu Zhitian's school. This time, when she performed in Beijing, she was heavily promoted by several wealthy people, and de Gopeira was led by these wealthy people when he visited the Star Theatre that day to appreciate the graceful demeanor of this typical Suzhou woman.

Liking to Stay in Bed

— Chuan Yizhi

The light yellow morning sun slants onto the upper end of the wall across from my garret, indicating that it is already past seven o'clock; although the warmth in the worn-out quilt feels very tempting, I dare not let go and close my drowsy eyes again, because I am concerned about the eight o'clock morning class, fearing that if I fall asleep, I will delay the classes of all the young ladies.

However, although my eyes are forced to open, my body is always lazy and unwilling to "move the venue," as if sleeping a little longer would be like taking a "Shiquan Dabu Wan" (Ten-Ingredient Tonic Pill) or getting a "blood-boosting shot," which would definitely restore the fatigue of yesterday's all-day work.

The morning sun on the upper end of the wall gradually moves to the window lattice below, as if telling me: this is already the time to continue forward on your life journey. It—the morning sun is what I consider the only accurate clock; although it will hide on cloudy and rainy days, making me unable to distinguish between early and late, I must wipe my face, brush my teeth, and put on my clothes; I must also run that mile-long road—a road full of chamber pots and vendors, in that tense battlefield of life, which is unwilling to let me, a wounded soldier, "go AWOL." Naturally, I cannot but clench my teeth, throw aside this lover—the worn-out quilt—that has followed me for seven or eight years, and jump up to catch up with the team in the midst of bugle calls.

Those who return from dancing late at night, sleeping head-to-head with their beloved wives, are the favored children of heaven, the uncrowned kings; at the same time, they are also obstacles in the path of human evolution. In this society that is actively brewing drastic changes, they are the last batch of those who are infatuated with a life of leisure, I have cursed them in this way. But, humans seem to exist for enjoyment, and if they have a moment to spare, they want even more comfort; I am still reluctant to part with this warm worn-out quilt, how can I blame them for indulging in their inherent happiness?

If I had a life that was more superior than reality, or equal to theirs, I would have to give them more sympathy, would this idea be wrong?

The Difficulty of Opening the City God Temple and Yu Garden

— Gao Yahun

The Yu Garden of the Shanghai City God Temple was originally divided into the Inner Garden, Outer Garden, and Dianchun Hall. The Outer Garden is the Nine-Bend Bridge and other places we often visit. The Inner Garden and Dianchun Hall are not often open. They are only opened during major festivals such as the Mid-Autumn Festival and the Dragon Boat Festival, allowing visitors to enter and tour. At other times, the double doors are tightly closed, and those who do not know people or have power are not allowed to enter and sightsee. It is a waste that such a great garden cannot be publicly exhibited and is only for the enjoyment of one or two private individuals. In 1929, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau once proposed to open Yu Garden for public enjoyment, but the result was not realized. A few days ago, a foreign engineer from the Municipal Works Bureau happened to be in the mood for a garden tour, so he borrowed a few Chinese colleagues and went to the City God Temple to tour the Inner Garden, Outer Garden, and Dianchun Hall. He felt that the scenery was secluded and the decorations were pleasant. It was a pity to keep it closed like this. After returning, he suggested to the Works Bureau to find a way to open it for citizens to tour. The Works Bureau accepted the foreign engineer's proposal and convened a joint meeting with the Education Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Social Bureau to discuss the opening method. The results were reported to the municipal government for approval. If approved, they would proceed with the second step of the opening procedure. Who knew that the municipal government would review the old case files and find that the three houses in the Inner Garden, Outer Garden, and Dianchun Hall all had owners in charge, and there was also a sugar industry elementary school and the industry association in Dianchun Hall. If opened, there would definitely be problems first. Moreover, the houses in Yu Garden have been built for many years, some have not been repaired, and some are already collapsing. After opening, there would definitely be danger. In addition, the roads are narrow, and even in the widest places, there are only three feet of space. If it is made a public tourist area, there will be crowding if there are too many tourists. With these difficulties, the opening of the City God Temple and Yu Garden was invisibly cancelled and became a permanently secret scenic spot.

Four Company Commanders in the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-One: Whispered Words Under the Lamp, Heartfelt Advice to a Weak Daughter; Walking with a Cane on the Mountain, Coldly Watching Heroes

While he was looking at the ground, he struggled hard, and blurted out a sentence, which was: Does Second Master only know this today? Ji Zhiyue was standing not far in front of him, but the sentence he said could not be heard clearly. However, it could be seen that he was deliberately using a question to evade the topic. Ji Zhiyue thought to himself, he is already troubled enough, things have come to this, it is almost like flowing water and falling flowers, spring is gone. Today, I blocked him until dark, so what? So he smiled at him: Since I returned to Haidian, I have been thinking of visiting your residence and thanking the Zhao family's old master. Unexpectedly, my elder brother's illness has been lingering on and on without any sign of improvement. I have to take care of things inside and out, and I can't spare an hour or two. So one day passed after another, and this matter was delayed. If I have time tomorrow or the day after, I will definitely come to your residence to visit. Go back and please say hello to Madam for me, goodbye! After saying this, he put on his hat and walked away with a bow. Gui Zhi stood in the same place, not leaving an inch, turning around and just looking at Ji Zhiyue's back. Later, two children from the neighborhood ran to her side and asked: Sister Yang, what are you doing standing here? Did you lose something? Gui Zhi then woke up and smiled: Isn't that right? I lost a small key. The two children actually believed it and started looking on the ground. Gui Zhi stopped them and said: Little brothers, don't look, I might have left this small key at home. So she stepped forward, touched the heads of the two children, and went home. Upon entering the door, she bumped into her mother, Jiang Shi. Seeing that Gui Zhi had quietly gone out earlier and now quietly returned, she couldn't help but feel suspicious, so she stared at her face. Seeing that her face was red, she felt even more uneasy, so she said: Your health hasn't been very good these past few days, so rest more at home. The weather is also very cool, don't go out and catch a cold again. (279)

Fiction

Feeble Cries

— Zhu Xiang

(1) Can You Bear to Call Me "Mr."?

Dear Wife:

Can you bear to call me "Mr."? Yes, in the past—five years ago—we used to call each other "Mr." and "Ms." for a while, but what is our relationship now? You are my wife, I am your husband, the father and mother of Yu'er—can you bear to call me "Mr."?

Ever since I came back from the shop the day before yesterday and saw Yu'er crying alone in the room, her eyes swollen and her voice hoarse, I was very surprised! Later, I also saw that your clothes were all gone. At first, I thought you had gone to a relative's house in a fit of anger, but I held Yu'er and went to inquire at every house, my legs were sore and my mouth was hoarse, running from dusk until midnight, and I still didn't see you. Yu'er was in my arms, and although she was asleep because she was too tired, she would still call out "Mommy!" in her sleep! Alas, my dear, if you exchanged my position, I'm afraid you would also be heartbroken!

My dear, my inability to allow you to have a fake woolen coat is really because the business in the shop has been too bad this year. The salary is owed, how can I pre-pay? Because of the economic panic. The year before last, when you asked me to make a gray-backed cheongsam, didn't I immediately agree to you? You are an educated woman, I think you wouldn't divorce me just because of these material things! Yu'er has been running a fever because she hasn't seen you for five days. My dear, come back!

(2) Just Need a Mouthful of Food

Mr. So-and-So:

It has been almost a year since the Rose Store closed down that I have been unemployed. During this year, although I have been running around trying to find a job to make a living, the year is so bleak that all the shops are embracing a tight policy, only choosing to lay off batches of partners, and absolutely not hiring new partners. Even if a few new shops open, the paper notices from their preparatory offices are just posted, but the staff inside have already been internally determined. People like me who are not well-informed always come back disappointed after hearing the news and running there. However, the various living expenses of my family, such as food, clothing, and housing, cannot be stopped because I am unemployed. Alas! Although I have tried my best to save money during this year, I have been patching here and there, and it is terribly miserable!

Now you, Mr., are preparing for the "National Goods Shopping Mall." When I heard the news, it was really like finding a bright lamp in the vast dark night! Mr., aren't you very fond of me, and aren't you a universally admired charitable person? I don't know how many people are living off of you. Please have pity on me and give me some work! I dare not argue about the amount of salary, as long as you can give me a mouthful of food, I will be very grateful. Waiting for your reply, so that I can come to you in person for instruction...

(3) The Devil of Sickness Will Never Let You Go Just Because You Are Poor

Old Brother So-and-So:

I am really ashamed that I have not been able to return your loan earlier, but now my illness has still not healed. Of course, I cannot work, but I cannot but ask for a doctor; although Dr. Wang treats me specially, I still have to pay for the half-dollar fare and the medicine expenses at the pharmacy. Although the newspaper office where I work considers my situation and still pays me half of my salary so that I can receive a salary while lying down, I still have to pay for medical expenses in addition to the daily expenses of the family. It is really a stretch, and I cannot make ends meet. However, if I don't see a doctor, it will really affect my life; if I see a doctor, I don't have the money. Being sick when you are poor is really the most bitter and miserable thing, but the hateful devil of sickness will not entangle you just because you are a poor person! Old brother, you are my most intimate friend, please help me with some material help...

In this bleak year, such tragic letters are often found in society. Then, what kind of influence this faint cry can have on those who hear it is within an unknowable number. However, although the effect of the cry is unknowable, the cry of the cry is still permeating society, this is the so-called modern scene!

Education News from Other Places

Jiangsu Province Plans to Issue Education Funds

The Jiangsu Provincial Middle School and Normal School have been notified that the funds for the first half of October have been issued (the Rural Normal School and Experimental Elementary School are for the first half of November, the Vocational School and Social Education Institutions are for the second half of October). The funds have been issued by the Education Funds Management Office and can now be collected separately. It is reported that the Education Funds Management Office, in addition to issuing the funds for this half month, the winter study abroad funds, and two months of food expenses for the normal schools, now has about 50,000 yuan in its treasury. To continue issuing the funds for the second half of the month, it is still short 90,000 yuan. It is now issuing orders to various counties and sending personnel to urge the payment of land tax and slaughter tax. The fund issuance notification for the second half of October for middle schools and normal schools (the second half of November for rural normal schools and experimental elementary schools, the first half of November for social education and vocational schools) will be issued within this month. However, as the Gregorian New Year approaches, banks will be closed for business. The funds will be received by various schools around January 1. The Jiangsu Education Funds Audit Committee held a meeting yesterday and signed the fund issuance notification for the first half of November for middle schools and normal schools (the first half of December for rural normal schools and experimental elementary schools, the second half of November for social education and vocational education). It was sent to the Education Department for stamping on the 27th. The schools hope to receive the funds for this half month before the winter vacation on January 18. The issuance of this notification must wait until the above-mentioned half-month fund notification (the second half of October for middle schools, the second half of November for rural normal schools and experimental elementary schools) has been received before it can be issued, around the beginning of January. It is also reported that the Management Office borrowed 400,000 yuan from various counties for this year's winter irrigation. Due to the impact of the current situation, it was not possible to do so immediately. Now, the first batch of counties has reported that they can borrow approximately tens of thousands of yuan. Only half of the funds have been transferred to the treasury, about 70,000 yuan. They are currently being urged separately. It is expected that the funds for the half-month to be issued within this month and the half-month funds before the winter vacation on January 18 will not have any problems.

Zhejiang Education Department Orders Promulgation of Method for Spot-Checking Elementary School Students' Grades

Spot-checking is divided into total testing, temporary testing, and joint testing

The Zhejiang Education Department believes that the methods for spot-checking elementary school grades in various counties and cities in the province are inconsistent and the standards are different, and there should be unified regulations. Since the Ministry of Education temporarily exempted the elementary school graduation examinations, it is even more necessary for various counties and cities to universally conduct spot-checks to rectify the academic performance of elementary school students. The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department has specially ordered the promulgation of an outline of the Zhejiang Provincial Method for Spot-Checking the Academic Performance of Elementary School Students in Various Counties and Cities, ordering uniform compliance. The outline of the method is recorded below: 1. The Education Department, in order to rectify the academic performance of elementary school students in various counties and cities, specially formulates the Zhejiang Provincial Method for Spot-Checking the Academic Performance of Elementary School Students in Various Counties and Cities. All counties and cities must conduct spot-checks in accordance with this method outline. 2. Each county and city will conduct the examination separately for students in the third grade and above. 3. The schools, grades, and subjects to be spot-checked will be determined by each county and city based on the results of the inspection, and those deemed necessary will be examined. A total spot-check of the entire county and city may also be conducted in light of the circumstances of each county and city. 4. When conducting spot-checks, each county and city should have the inspectors conduct them temporarily while inspecting each school. However, they may also gather students of the same grade from nearby schools to conduct the examination together in one place. 5. The test questions for the spot-check subjects and the standards for grading the results will be handled by the staff of the Education Bureau in each county and city, who will be responsible for organizing the Elementary School Student Performance Spot-Check Committee. If a total spot-check of the entire county and city is conducted, the members of this committee may hire a number of people who are not related to the schools being spot-checked to serve as members. 6. After conducting the spot-check, if any county or city finds that the performance of all students in a grade in a certain subject is too poor, the school should be warned to find ways to remedy it and urged to improve. 7. After the end of each semester, each county and city should submit a list to the Education Department for record, detailing the schools, grades, number of people, subjects, total scores, and handling process of the spot-checks conducted in a semester. 8. The detailed spot-check methods should be formulated by each county and city and submitted to the Education Department for record. 9. The expenses used for handling spot-check matters in each county and city will be paid from the education funds of each county and city. 10. This method outline will be implemented from the date of its formulation and promulgation by the Education Department.

Jidda Middle School Department Resumes Classes Yesterday

The Middle School Principal Position Temporarily Held Concurrently by President Zheng

Director Pan Issues Statement Hoping for Proper Handling

(China and Foreign News Agency) According to reports, a disturbance occurred in the Jidda University Department in West Shanghai. This agency's reporter specially drove to Zhenru yesterday to investigate. It was learned that the cause of the disturbance was purely due to external incitement, resulting in a sudden strike. However, after only one day, the situation took a sharp turn for the better. President Zheng Hongnian issued two notices, and students voluntarily resumed classes. When the reporter arrived at the school, order had already returned to normal, and the sounds of reading were heard again. Zheng also reported the resumption of classes to the Ministry of Education. The so-called fleeting disturbance has come to an end. The texts of Zheng's notices are recorded below:

Notice One Regarding the matter of this notice: Since Mr. Kuang Songling has been in charge of the Middle School Department of this school, he has carried out reforms and rectifications, and the teaching and management have been strict, and the discipline has been excellent. This president has been very pleased with this. Unexpectedly, a few students were suddenly incited by unscrupulous elements outside the school the day before yesterday, causing an incident, which is truly distressing. It must be known that young people are full of vitality and easily agitated. Director Kuang has always been earnest in his hopes for the students, and his reprimands may have been overly strict. However, my students should understand his good intentions and encourage themselves even more. How can they recklessly listen to others and indulge their nature? Impulsively, they acted according to their likes and dislikes, not hesitating to create unnecessary problems. One person sang, and a hundred followed, eventually turning wrong into right. The central government has repeatedly issued orders to rectify education. At a time when the situation is turbulent, the security of Shanghai is particularly important. This president cannot bear to see a very small number of my students implicate the majority of the innocent. Moreover, the Middle School Department of this school has a long history, and this president has laid the foundation and expanded it later, and the relationship is extremely close. Therefore, I cannot let go. From this day forward, all the powers and responsibilities of the Middle School Principal will be temporarily held concurrently by this president until Director Kuang returns to school. I hope that all students will concentrate on their studies, and all disputes will be handled carefully by this president. This president has always been warm-hearted in his care for students. If there are still those who are obstinate and disregard the overall situation, then the school rules are in place, and it will not be difficult to use them to enforce discipline. Let each of you be respectful of this notice.

Notice Two Regarding the matter of this notice: The Middle School Department of this school has recently experienced some disturbances, which are currently being handled personally by this president. All my teachers and staff, who hold leadership positions, should each take responsibility and set an example. Please do not be absent without reason or leave your posts without permission. In addition to the Registration Office strictly verifying attendance, this notice is hereby issued.

(Shanghai News Agency) The Affiliated Middle School of National Jidda University experienced a situation where a portion of students, dissatisfied with the strict policies of the Middle School Principal Kuang Songling, surrounded the principal and expelled teachers and staff the day before yesterday morning. The situation was extremely serious at one point. After President Zheng issued a notice and reprimanded the students yesterday, the situation has eased, and students are attending classes as usual. Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau also issued a statement. The details are recorded below:

Cause of the Incident According to Shanghai News Agency reporters, the cause of this disturbance is that the Middle School Principal Kuang Songling has been extremely strict in managing students on weekdays, and he often checks students' correspondence, which has led to opposition from some students and the brewing of this disturbance.

Truth of the Outbreak At 9:00 AM on the 26th, when the first class was over and the second class was about to begin, suddenly a group of about 20 to 30 students surrounded the principal's office and various department offices, expelling a small number of teachers and staff. However, it was found that only a small number of high school and normal school students participated at the time, and most of the other students did not participate, and there were no rude or barbaric actions, nor were there any incidents of holding copper pillars or iron axes as weapons.

Classes Resume as Usual After the incident occurred, President Zheng arrived at the school that afternoon and severely reprimanded the students, immediately restoring order. Students resumed self-study as usual in the evening, and classes have also resumed as usual since 9:00 AM yesterday. However, a small number of teachers and staff have not yet returned to school, and President Zheng has sent letters to inform them. Before Middle School Principal Kuang Songling returns to school, all principal duties will be temporarily held concurrently by President Zheng.

Director Pan's Statement Yesterday, Shanghai News Agency reporters visited Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau and asked for his opinion on this case. Director Pan immediately stated that he was deeply saddened to learn about the disturbance at the Affiliated Middle School of Jidda University as reported in today's newspapers. The Education Bureau is currently sending personnel to investigate this case. He sincerely hopes that the school authorities, for the sake of rectifying discipline, should assess the students' likes and dislikes and handle the matter properly. At the same time, they should prioritize the students' studies and not allow the affairs of a few people to affect the studies of the entire student body. This is what he particularly hopes for, he said.

Zhejiang University Basketball Team Defeats St. John's in Friendly Match

Zhejiang University's Passing and Shooting Were Excellent

Result: 42 to 36

After the Zhejiang University basketball team arrived in Shanghai, they played their first match against St. John's University last night, held in the St. John's Recreation Room. Due to the dim lighting and poor visibility, movement was affected. Zhejiang University relied on Miao Mei's short passes and accurate shooting to defeat St. John's 42 to 36. However, the score fluctuated during the match, and the situation was quite tense.

The entire Zhejiang University team was balanced, with good offense and defense. Wang Di'an and Qi Guangyu's shots were accurate and confident. Wang Pusheng's support made the whole team work seamlessly, and Shi Hengyuan's defense was well-positioned and controlled. The team has made a lot of progress compared to when they came to Shanghai last winter. Their victory over St. John's was not accidental. St. John's lost because their defense was weak, their coordination was unfamiliar, and their shooting was inaccurate. They were fortunate to lose by only six points.

One-Point Difference After the referee Shen Siliang ordered the game to begin, Qi Guangyu of Zhejiang University scored the first point. Zhou Xuexian of St. John's made a layup under the basket, tying the score 2-2. After that, Zhejiang University's momentum increased, and their shots were accurate. The score became 8-4 and 12-6. Zhou Du of St. John's called a timeout to boost morale. Tao Zunan, Zhou Xuexian, and Wu Youliang each scored, making the score 12-12. The situation became tense. From then on, the score was very close, and it was difficult to tell who had the advantage. Wang Di'an of Zhejiang University scored on a free throw against Tao Zuran, taking the lead again 13-12. Ma Fangcui of St. John's made a layup, making the score 14-13. St. John's took the lead for the first time. However, Zhejiang University coordinated their offense, and their formation was tight. Wang Di'an scored repeatedly, taking the lead again 21-16. St. John's made every effort to counterattack. Zhou Xuexian made three shots in a row, and the situation suddenly changed again. St. John's took a slight lead with a score of 22-21.

Turning Defeat into Victory After the first half ended, Wu Zhiyi replaced Ma Fangcui for St. John's. After Shi Hengyuan of Zhejiang University scored the first point, Wu and Zhang of St. John's scored in a row, adding six points. St. John's took the lead for the second time with a score of 28-23. However, St. John's passes were often ineffective after that, and there was no one to receive them. In addition, Zhejiang University's defenses were tight, and there was no room to take advantage of. As a result, it became Zhejiang University's game. Qi Guangyu's aim was accurate, and he made many contributions. In a short time, he scored five goals. St. John's had just risen to the blue sky and was hit hard again, falling behind 28-38. At this time, St. John's lineup was like a plate of scattered sand, while Zhejiang University's work was meticulous. Success or failure seemed to have been decided in secret. St. John's reorganized their troops and persevered. Zhou Xuexian and Ma Fangcui each made shots, but the gains did not make up for the losses. In the end, they lost 36-42. Zhejiang University will play against Western Youth at 8:20 PM tonight at the Western Youth Basketball Gym.

Tonight: Pu Cheng vs. Mai Ling; Liang Hua vs. Shanghai University, Liang Hua Requests Postponement

Liang Hua's defeat was particularly regrettable. They broke through Mai Ling's defense in the first half and led all the way until 25 to 31. He scored two goals in a row, and because of his brilliant pass, Liu Zhenyuan followed up and scored. In an instant, they scored eight points in a row, and Liang Hua took the lead 16-13. As a result, Liang Hua took the lead with a difference of three or four points. Although Mai Ling briefly took the lead with 24-23, Liang Hua still defeated Mai Ling 27-26 in the first half.

Generals Ejected Starting in the second half, Liang Hua was still in the lead, but the situation gradually deteriorated. Center Li Huizhong and rear guards Zhang Jingshi and Yin Hongxiang each had three fouls recorded. Sure enough, Yin Hongxiang was ejected when the score was 35-32. Mai Ling added one point. One minute later, Zhang Jingshi was also ejected. Mai Ling added another point. Liang Hua was shaken from then on and could not support themselves. Mai Ling scored eight points in a row, taking the lead 39-35. However, Liang Hua continued to fight and actually tied the score at 41-41. Mai Ling quickly started using fresh troops in a rotation, and from then on Liang Hua collapsed. As a result, Mai Ling won 54-41.

Aftermath After the battle, the spectators, seeing Liang Hua's regrettable defeat, blamed the referee for being unfair. The Westerners were fine, and no one dared to take action. Wu Jiatang was attacked by punches and kicks, but fortunately he escaped, otherwise the consequences would have been unthinkable. How emotional the spectators were!

Date… January 29th to February 2nd

Address… Shanghai Rifle Shooting Club, No. 3 Beijing Road

The Sino-British International Rifle Shooting Competition in this city started in March this year. The Chinese team consisted of five members: Li Gongxian, Shen Lince, Zhang Yingda, Liu Zongfu, and Xu Shizhang.
