Transportation

Vehicles: The vehicles currently owned by the railway were purchased with the construction capital of the Jiangshan-Lanxi section, totaling nine locomotives, thirty passenger cars, and eighty freight cars. Those purchased with the construction capital of the Jinhua-Yushan section, i.e., ordered with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity, totaled six locomotives, twenty-four passenger car underframes, and fifty freight car underframes. Currently, except for the fifty freight car underframes, which arrived in October and have been assembled and can be added to transport, only one locomotive can arrive this year. The remaining five locomotives and twenty-four passenger car underframes are expected to arrive next spring.

Stations: There are a total of 36 stations on the entire railway. Zhakou and Sanlangmiao stations are specially set up to facilitate passengers and freight crossing the river and are limited to business operations. Those in the Jiangshan-Lanxi section include Jingjiang, Jiangbian, Lushan, Bailutang, Linpu, Jianshan, Meichi, Zhibu, Baimen, Zhuji, Paitou, Anhua, Suixi, Yiwu, Yiting, Xiaoshun, Tangya, Jinhua, Zhuma Pavilion, and Lanxi, totaling 20 stations. Those in the Jinhua-Yushan section include Gufang, Yangxi, Huzhen, Longyou, Anren, Zhangshutan, Quzhou, Erlishijie, Houxijie, Jiangshan, Hecun, Xintangbian, Xiazhen, and Yushan, totaling 14 stations.

Train Services: Currently, there are two direct passenger trains running back and forth each day on the Jiangshan-Lanxi section, and one mixed train running back and forth between Jiangbian and Jinhua. Between Jinhua and Quzhou, material trains are temporarily used to carry passengers and freight. After the opening of the entire line on December 28, there will be two direct passenger trains running back and forth each day between Jiangbian and Yushan, and one mixed train running back and forth each day between Jiangbian and Jinhua, Jinhua and Yushan, and Jinhua and Lanxi.

Organization

The railway engineering bureau originally had two departments: engineering and general affairs. The director of the bureau also served as the chief engineer, and the deputy director served as the director of general affairs. There were also secretaries, section chiefs, and division chiefs. Due to austerity, the two departments were abolished and replaced by four sections: general affairs, engineering, transportation, and accounting. The secretary was also dismissed. The general affairs section was divided into five subsections: documentation, materials, land and fields, general affairs, and personnel. The materials subsection managed material factories and locations. The engineering section was divided into three subsections: design, bridges, and construction, and also directed the first, second, and third main engineering sections. The transportation section was divided into three subsections: train operations, locomotive operations, and police affairs. Train, locomotive, and police affairs were each divided into sections, all under the jurisdiction of their respective managing subsections. The locomotive operations subsection, in addition to managing its sections, also managed the machine factory, the vehicle maintenance facility, and the locomotive materials depot. The accounting section was divided into three subsections: comprehensive review, inspection, and cashier.

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and Highways (Ti Cheng)

The original route of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, from Hangzhou upwards, was originally along the west bank of the Fuchun River through Tonglu and Jiande counties to reach Lanxi. Due to the difficulty of the project and the high cost, there was a proposal to change the route. In the winter of the 18th year, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway was stalled, and Chairman Zhang of the provincial government transferred colleagues from the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway to build the Xiaoshan-Jinhua-Lanxi-Changshan highway. Because the terrain along the line was flat, the Construction Department, with the approval of the provincial government, decided to convert this route into a light railway. The Xiaochang highway had long been designated as the main trunk line in the hinterland of the province. Now that it has been converted into a railway, the highway route has had to be changed accordingly. The current fourth trunk line of the new highway network plan in the province, the Hangguang Line, 丨丨 which is a section of the third trunk line of the Seven-Province Highway, the Hu-Gui Line, 丨丨 the reason for extending the Hangfu Road to Lanxi is for this reason. This exchange history of this section of the route is the beginning of the relationship between the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the highway. Now that the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has officially opened to traffic on the entire line, the Hangzhou-Guangdong highway project has also been completed section by section. Looking back on the day of completion, recalling the decision to change the route in the 18th year, which allowed the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway to be completed quickly, although the highway felt a little difficult, there was not much obstacle to progress. It can be seen that the provincial and department heads weighed the priorities and appropriate actions that day, and it is also worth commemorating that the railway and highway can exchange routes to express the spirit of mutual assistance.

After the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway changed its route, Xixing became the starting point of the entire line due to the separation of the Qiantang River. The river is vast and cannot be easily dredged. The transportation of passengers and goods is inconvenient. On the highway side, Zhejiang's east and west could not be connected because of the Qiantang River. Therefore, the need for the Qiantang River Bridge is shared by both the railway and the highway, and it is urgently needed. Fortunately, with the approval of the provincial government, the Construction Department has been committed to the grand vision of developing eastern Zhejiang. It has entrusted experts to carefully study the design of the Qiantang River Bridge and stipulated that the railway and highway should run on the same bridge. The transportation revenue is used as a guarantee for the bridge construction cost. Therefore, the cooperation between the railway and the highway is closer because of the Qiantang River Bridge. In the future, the prosperity of the economy and society in eastern Zhejiang will advance with the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and highway business, which can be predicted.

Since the opening of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the number of people crossing the Qiantang River by ferry has increased day by day, reaching more than 400,000 people per month. However, the ferry equipment is simple, and the western and docks have not yet been built, making it inconvenient for travelers. Although the Qiantang River Bridge has been designed, it is slow to solve the urgent need, and the ferry still needs to be improved. According to the current plan, in addition to reorganizing the existing docks and ferries, it is planned to start the construction of the Hanyang dock immediately. The funding has also been stipulated to be borne jointly by the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau, the Highway Bureau, and local people. The day of construction will not be far away. This is a facility that the province should have to facilitate transportation on both sides of the river before the Qiantang River Bridge is built, and the railway and highway authorities especially hope for its early success.

The nature of highways is to supplement the shortcomings of railway transportation. Since Zhejiang Province has the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and is urgently seeking the development of eastern Zhejiang, all highway plans should be based on this principle and strive to assist the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and develop together within the possible scope. Now, the major stations of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway are connected to highway lines. Let's list them below:

(1) Xiaoshan Station: The highways that connect to Xiaoshan, such as the Xiaoshao, Shao Cao Sheng, and Sheng Xin sections, all rely on this station to connect with the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, which is the hub for Shaoxing to use the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. (2) Zhuji Station: This station is connected to the Shao-Zhuji road to facilitate transportation to Shaoxing. (3) Yiwu Station: This station is connected to the Yi-Dong road, and then through Dongyang via Changle to connect to Sheng County and transfer to Taizhou, so that all parts of Taizhou enjoy the convenience of railway transportation. Furthermore, counties in Ningbo can also reach Xinchang via the Fengxin road, and then through the Shengxin and Shengchang roads to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway.

(4) Jinhua Station: This station is connected to the Jin-Yong, Yong Jin, and Jin-Li roads to reach counties under the jurisdiction of Lishui. Roads under the jurisdiction of Lishui, such as the Li-Yun, Long Li Qing, and Wen roads, are all under construction. After completion in the future, Wenzhou and Lishui will be connected to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway through Jinhua.

(5) Lanxi Station: This station can be connected to Jiande, Dun'an, and Suian counties to reach the border.

(6) Longyou Station: From this station, go through Xikou in Longyou to reach Suichang and Songyang, and then connect to the counties under the jurisdiction of Lishui.

(7) Quzhou Station:

(8) Jiangshan Station: From these two stations, you can rely on the connection of the Qu-Chang, Chang Yu, Qu-Jiang, and Jiang-Guang Jiang Pu roads to directly reach Yushan and Guangfeng in Jiangxi and Pucheng and Jianou in Fujian. The well-connected transportation of Quzhou has the effect of surrounding and supporting the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. The above roads may be completed, not completed, under construction, or under planning. All highway colleagues are working to implement the provincial and department officials' intention to develop eastern Zhejiang and assist the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. As for the Quzhou-Lanxi and Quzhou-Jiangshan sections, although some sections are parallel to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, Quzhou is an important military town, and it is necessary to add a transportation auxiliary line. Moreover, during the construction of the Jinhua-Yushan section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, these two sections of the highway had already been completed, which greatly facilitated the transportation of all materials and the transfer of employees. The early completion of the Jinhua-Yushan section was also due to the Quzhou-Lanxi and Quzhou-Jiangshan highways. Even after the entire Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is opened to traffic, it can rely on short-distance business to maintain itself and achieve complementary effects. There is no competition.

Since the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the highway have the same mission of developing eastern Zhejiang, it is expected that the production of various places in eastern Zhejiang will increase and transportation will be more frequent in the future. Although the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has been opened to traffic and the new highway network plan in this province will soon be completed, the operation methods still need to be improved. It is hoped that the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the highway will today discuss and agree on a proper intermodal transport method, so that the great event of developing eastern Zhejiang will have a greater effect. This is also a major task that the railway and highway colleagues should work together on.

As the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway holds its opening ceremony, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau will compile and publish a special publication, and I was asked to contribute an article. I believe that the province has railways. Except for Guangdong and the three northeastern provinces, only Zhejiang has it now. The great achievements of past chairmen and department heads are well-known to the people of Zhejiang and do not need my words. Furthermore, the Chinese people are allowed to build railways themselves. After the Ping-Sui Railway, only the current Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway exists. Director Du diligently handled the matter from beginning to end, and the contributions of the colleagues involved are also well-known to the people of Zhejiang and do not need my words. What I want to say is something else. I have been in charge of the provincial highway bureau for many years, and highways are inherently supplementary to railway transportation. At this time, when the provincial and department officials are actively developing eastern Zhejiang, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the highway share this mission. Therefore, the past relationship, future cooperation, and current connection between the two parties are what I should say. What do the people of Zhejiang and the colleagues of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau think?

Guide to Ceremony Program and Sightseeing

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is scheduled to hold a full line opening ceremony in Jinhua at 2:00 PM on December 29, 1933. The Construction Department of Zhejiang Province has specially invited people from all walks of life to visit. The order of the opening ceremony is as follows:

Ceremony Program (1) Stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Bow three times to the Party and National Flags and the portrait of the Premier, (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will, (5) Two minutes of silence, (6) Chairman's opening speech, (7) Bureau chief's report, (8) Superior officer's instruction, (9) Guest speeches, (10) Photographing the opening of the railway.

Notes for Guests (1) Guests should gather at the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road Station of the Sanlang Temple in Hangzhou at 10:00 AM on December 28 and take a ferry to the Jiangbian (riverside) Station in Xixing; (2) At the reception desk at the Jiangbian Station, collect a commemorative badge for the full line opening of the railway, which will be used to board the special train; (3) The special train is scheduled to depart from Jiangbian at 8:00 AM on the same day to Jinhua for the ceremony; (4) On the morning of December 29, at 7:00 AM, take the train from Jinhua to visit the along the Jinyu section; (5) Guests who participate in the opening ceremony in Jinhua and do not go to Yushan may take the special train back to Hangzhou that night; (6) The special train will provide meals and lunch at Jinhua Station.

Scenic Spots Along the Line The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway line has beautiful mountains and rivers, and the scenery is outstanding. Near Xiaoshan Station, there are scenic spots such as Xiang Lake, Yue Wang City, Yilan Pavilion, and Xianyan Mountain; at Zhuji Station, there is the Ningluo Village, which is the Washing Silk Creek of Xi Shi; other places such as Jia Yan and Wu Xie have clear streams and quiet temples, with unique charm, and the waterfalls are majestic, with the natural sounds of nature. Near Jinhua Station, there are scenic spots such as Beishan and Fangyan, with many peaks surrounded by greenery, pools, waterfalls, and caves. The Taoist books refer to this place as the Thirty-Six Cave Heavens. Other places such as Jiufeng Mountain, Sandieyan, and Xiaonanhai are all located between Lanxi and Longyou. Near Jiangshan Station, there is the magnificent Xianxia Mountain, and the stone steps of Xianxia Pass winding like a long snake, which is truly spectacular. Half a kilometer from Yushan Station, there are scenic spots such as Wuan Mountain and Heling Temple. Travelers along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway should not miss visiting these places. Transportation Facilities and Management Policies of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway

— Jin Shi Kuan

(1) Introduction

The mission of Zhejiang Province in building the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is to facilitate the transportation of people and develop the economy of the interior. With its completion, it will run through Zhejiang Province and connect Jiangxi and Fujian. Its economic mission is undoubtedly significant, and it also occupies an important position in politics and military affairs. We are operating this railway to seek the development of business and transportation, to ensure that the people along the line receive the greatest convenience and benefits, and to ensure that the railway itself not only balances its income and expenditure but also has a surplus to repay the principal. All colleagues serving on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway can recognize this point and strive not to fail the mission of building this railway.

Although the Jinhua-Yushan section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has just been completed, the Hangzhou-Jiangbian to Lanxi section has been in operation for more than two years. The transportation facilities and management policies of the Jiang-Lan section in the past two years have also been quite different from those of other railways in our country. After the full line is opened to traffic, we should continue to implement this policy and make changes. I hope that experts from all walks of life can teach us.

(2) Regarding Transportation Facilities

(1) Emphasize Third-Class Passenger Cars Most railways have passenger classes divided into three or four classes. Passenger revenue, however, shows that the third and fourth classes account for almost 90% of the total. Therefore, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway recognizes this point and puts its full spirit into organizing third-class passenger cars. The air, light, and cleanliness facilities are all above those of other railways, which is generally acknowledged.

(2) Operating Small Worker Trains in Winter The Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway all operates fourth-class cars to benefit ordinary people. Although the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway does not have this facility, it specially operates worker trains in winter because many people along the line go out to work and return to their hometowns in winter. Its nature is no different from the fourth class of other railways.

(3) Third-Class Chinese Dining Cars Most railways use Western-style cuisine for passenger food facilities, which not only promotes foreign goods but also has expensive prices and does not conform to Chinese habits, making passengers feel inconvenienced. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway does not sell Western food and divides Chinese food into three grades to facilitate passengers of all levels. In addition, it cancels the peddling of miscellaneous foods in third-class cars to maintain order.

(4) Adding Second and Third-Class Sleeping Cars The sleeping car facilities on various railways are limited to the first and second classes. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is now adding second and third-class sleeping cars to facilitate night train passengers.

B. Freight

From the perspective of the railway's business itself, developing freight transportation is even more important than passenger transportation. Because the equipment cost of passenger transportation is greater than that of freight transportation, the development of freight transportation should be especially noted. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway's development of freight transportation facilities can also be divided into the following points:

(1) Implementing Responsible Transportation The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway handled responsible transportation from the beginning of freight transportation, initially with limited regulations. Since July 1933, the railway has been fully responsible for the goods, and compensation will be paid according to regulations if there is any loss. However, since its implementation, there have been very few compensation matters, which shows that responsible transportation is not difficult to handle, as long as the management procedures of the employees are complete. Moreover, responsible transportation does not increase prices, as it is considered the responsibility of the railway bureau.

(2) Expanding the Scope of Freight Transportation The methods are divided into the following points:

(1) The places through which the railway line passes are not all famous cities and towns, so it is necessary to find ways to absorb goods from farther away. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has built connecting docks or sidings at Xiaoshan, Linpu, Yiwu, Jinhua, and Lanxi stations, directly reaching the waterfront and implementing water-land connection transportation.

(2) At the Sanlang and Zhakou docks in Hangzhou, stations are set up separately to carry goods and handle ferry procedures.

(3) It is planned to set up business offices in the center of the city to receive goods and transport them to the station on behalf of the merchants. These are all methods to facilitate merchants and expand the scope of freight transportation.

(3) Commercializing Freight Transportation Methods Most of China's railways are government-run and have a monopoly nature, so business methods inevitably become stained with officialdom habits. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway starts from commercial principles in its business, on the one hand, correcting the way employees treat merchants, and on the other hand, imparting railway transportation knowledge to passengers and merchants. The implementation methods are: one is to print the railway transportation regulations into advertisements and post them everywhere, even in various towns along the line, to avoid the transfer company from manipulating them. The second is to give merchants the opportunity to express their opinions, convene transportation conferences in important cities along the line, and the railway bureau and merchants jointly discuss and communicate their opinions. The third is to train employees and pay attention to business habits, and treat merchants with a peaceful and sincere attitude.

C. Intermodal Transportation

The joint passenger transportation method between the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway has been implemented since January 1932. The responsible freight intermodal transportation method was implemented in July 1933. The midway formalities can be avoided, and the commission of the transfer company can be saved. The burden on merchants is reduced, the sales of goods are increased, and the railway business is also increased. After the full line is opened to traffic, it is planned to join the national intermodal transportation, and freight transportation will surely improve. For example, paper products along the line can be directly transported to the north. As for the intermodal transportation with the highways connected to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, such as the Xiaoshao, Jinyongwu, Yidong, and Jiangpu roads, we are separately discussing the methods. However, water-land intermodal transportation cannot be realized for a while because the waterways and ships do not have a formal organization.

D. Business Conditions

The business income of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway in 1932 was more than 1.26 million yuan, of which 600,000 yuan was in the first half of the year and 660,000 yuan in the second half of the year, with an average increase of 10,000 yuan per month. At the beginning of 1933, from July to October 1933, the average monthly income was 120,000 yuan, an increase of 20% compared with the second half of 1932. It can be said that there will be an increase when the Jinyu section is opened to traffic in the future. As for the number of passengers, there were 970,000 people in 1932, with an average of 80,000 people per month. In January of this year, the number of passengers exceeded 100,000 after the worker's car was added. The tonnage of freight, excluding engineering and official cargo, was 68,000 tons in 1932, of which 25,000 tons were in the second half of last year and 43,000 tons were in the first half of this year. The increase in tonnage is quite large, which shows that more and more merchants are using railway transportation.

E. Developing the Local Economy

The purpose of developing transportation is not only to make it conform to economic principles, but also to bear the mission of developing the agricultural, industrial, and commercial industries in the places it passes through, so that they can support each other. Railways in various countries have organizations to study, investigate, and revitalize the industries along the line. The South Manchurian and Central Eastern Railways also used this method, and their businesses have developed. Although the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway does not have the spare capacity to directly support the development of agriculture, industry, and commerce along the line, we have investigated the economic situation in various places and found several points that can be reported:

(1) The population along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is quite dense, and the products are not self-sufficient. People often go to work in the Hangzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou area and return to their hometowns in winter to spend the year, so there is a mobile nature.

(2) The economic situation along the line is still the organization of the rural society. The products are mostly agricultural products and livestock. The exported goods, in addition to rice, are mostly by-products such as pigs and cattle. The imported goods, in Hangzhou, are natural fertilizers collected from Jiaxing, Huzhou, Suzhou, and Changzhou, as well as foreign goods such as cotton yarn, cloth, kerosene, sugar, and fertilizers. In the Ningbo-Shaoxing area, they are salt, cotton yarn, and cloth. Most of them are raw materials for trading manufactured goods, and the value cannot be offset, which leads to the decline of the rural economy. Therefore, it is urgent to support the development of agriculture, industry, and commerce along the line.

(3) There are two inland commercial routes in the Jiangshan area of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, one to Fujian and the other to Jiangxi. The economic organization is similar to that of the Jinhua-Quzhou area, and it is also necessary to support its development.

(3) Regarding Management Policies

The key points of railway management are efficiency and economy. Based on these two objectives, the management policies of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway can be described in the following points:

(1) Adopting an Efficient Organization The organization of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau is simple and effective. Under the director, there are only four sections: General Affairs, Engineering, Transportation, and Accounting. After the opening of traffic, the three parts related to transportation, namely, car affairs, machinery affairs, and police affairs, are combined into a transportation section. The responsibility is specialized, the command is convenient, and cooperation is easy. The sections are divided into shares, with small scopes and few people.

(2) Strictly Implementing the Budget System To seek the economic management of the railway, the budget must be used as the standard for the allocation of funds. Since its opening, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has strictly implemented the budget system. All capital expenditures and business expenditures are specified in detail in advance. Since there is a fixed allocation standard for funds, the expenditure and income can be adapted, the debts can be repaid, and the credit can be maintained.

(3) Reducing the Business Percentage The business percentage is the ratio of expenditure to income. The business income of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway in 1932 was 1.26 million yuan, and the business expenditure was 880,000 yuan. The ratio of income to expenditure is less than 65%, and we must find ways to reduce it further. In China, the income-expenditure ratio of the Beining Railway is less than 50%, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is 65%, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway is 70%, and the South Manchurian Railway, which is operated by the Japanese, is 30%. This depends on whether the management is effective and economical. Now that the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is fully completed, the income will definitely increase, and the expenditure will definitely not increase in the same proportion. This can be asserted.

(4) Training Employees To increase the efficiency of railway management, we must first seek to improve the organization and supplement talent. After the opening of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, we recruited students with appropriate levels for the various positions needed in advance and set up three training classes for car affairs, machinery affairs, and police affairs, teaching practical courses and implementing strict operational training. Currently, 220 people have completed the training and have been assigned to serve. The completion of the Jinyu section and the fact that no new people have been appointed in the three parts of car machinery and police are also one of the innovations of this railway.

(5) Improving Police Efficiency The railway police were originally set up to maintain order, protect passengers and goods, and supplement the shortage of local police force. In addition to the aforementioned two duties, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Police can also check passenger tickets, which can save many station staff and improve their status. In addition, the railway police are ordered to guard the goods in place of the cargo porters. The police must also obey the command of the station chief to unify their authority. Therefore, the disadvantages of the police not listening to the station chief's command and conflicts with the car affairs staff have not been seen on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway.

The Operation of Railcars on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway

(4) The Experience of Jiang

Zhejiang Province's operation of railways is not the beginning of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan line. At the end of the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, the Zhejiang Railway Company was initiated, and the sections from Zhakou to Gongchen Bridge, Hangzhou to Fengjing, and Cao'e River to Ningbo were completed one after another. Zhejiang Province had such achievements as early as 25 years ago. Later, due to the Qing government's advocacy of national railway ownership and the high cost of the Zhejiang Railway itself, poor management, and inability to maintain it, the government took over in 1914, but the invested capital was not recovered. Now, under the guidance of the chief officer and the efforts of the responsible personnel, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has achieved considerable results in a short period of time and in an environment of economic difficulties, which has had a great impact on the future of China's railways. The currently commercially operated Wuzha Road, Yuping Road, Zhanglong Road, Tongpu Road, and Chengyu Road are all planning to follow the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway method and proceed actively in separate areas, changing the trend of national railway ownership and shifting the psychology of social construction difficulties. The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has made considerable contributions. From this, it can be seen that in China, where financial resources are difficult, only the central government can formulate principles. All national trunk lines and national defense border lines should be built by the central government as soon as possible, and the provincial lines should be given economic and technical assistance by the central government and handled by the provinces separately. Only through the cooperation of the central government and the provinces can China's railway construction be opened up and Mr. Sun Yat-sen's plan for 100,000 miles of railways be gradually completed. This is the feeling that Shixuan has gained from serving on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway.

The Future of Telephone Service along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway

— Zhao Zengjue

Railways, highways, and telecommunications all occupy the same position in transportation and bear the same mission, complementing each other and having their own special uses. Zhejiang Province has a considerable history in highways and telecommunications, and the scale can be said to be roughly complete. Now, the only state-owned railway in the country, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, is scheduled to hold a full line opening ceremony. I would like to make a brief contribution on the distribution of Zhejiang Province's long-distance telephone lines along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the future of the business:

The Zhejiang Province telecommunications network divides the province into seven major trunk lines: Hangzhou-Changxing, Hangzhou-Ningbo, Ningbo-Wenzhou, Hangzhou-Quzhou, Quzhou-Wenzhou, Hangzhou-Chuzhou, and Hangzhou-Fengjing. The Hangzhou-Changxing line passes through Yuhang, Wukang, Wuxing, and reaches Changxing, connecting Jiangsu to reach Nanjing. The Hangzhou-Ningbo line runs along the Hangzhou-Ningbo Road to Ningbo. The Ningbo-Wenzhou line passes through Ninghai, Linhai, Huangyan, Yueqing, and reaches Yongjia, which will be connected to Fujian in the future. The Hangzhou-Quzhou line runs along the Qiantang River, often connecting Changshan with Jiangxi. The Quzhou-Wenzhou line passes through Qu County, Longyou, Suichang, Songyang, Lishui, Qingtian, and reaches Yongjia. The Hangzhou-Chuzhou line passes through Hangzhou, along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road, through Jinhua, Wuyi, Yongkang, Jinyun, and reaches Lishui. The Hangzhou-Fengjing line runs from Hangzhou, along the Hangzhou-Shanghai Road, connecting Jiangsu to reach Shanghai. Therefore, the entire Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway line accounts for two of the province's long-distance telephone trunk lines: Hangzhou, passing through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Yiwu to reach Jinhua, is the first section of the Hangzhou-Chuzhou trunk line; Lanxi, passing through Longyou, Qu County, Jiangshan to reach Yushan, is the end section of the Hangzhou-Quzhou trunk line; Jinhua and Lanxi are connected by the Jinlan branch line. In addition, there are branch lines laid between Yiwu and Pujiang, Yiwu and Dongyang, Jinhua and Wuyi, Jinhua and Yongkang, Longyou and Suichang, Jiangshan and Changshan, and Lanxi and Tangxi. Therefore, wherever the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway reaches, not only can long-distance telephones be used, but it can also be connected to any of the 71 counties in the province that have long-distance telephones, as well as Beijing and Shanghai. Travelers in Zhejiang, thanks to the completion of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, can start from Qiantang in the morning and stay overnight in Xianxia; they can also use the dense Zhejiang telecommunications network to be able to confide in their family and children, even when they are thousands of miles away, to comfort the feelings of the traveler. ( )

In addition to the above-mentioned long-distance telecommunications network, there are urban telephone facilities in Jinhua, Lanxi, Qu County, Jiangshan, and other places along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. The telephone users in Jinhua and Lanxi are both around one or two hundred, all of which are operated by provincial funds. The urban telephones in Qu County and Jiangshan were originally prepared by the respective counties, but because of the construction of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, it is necessary to strive to expand them to meet the needs; however, due to the poor efficiency of the original components, it is difficult to maintain them, and they will also be transferred to the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau for takeover, in order to improve and facilitate the reorganization. The urban telephone in Longyou was not urgently needed, but recently it has also been affected by the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, and the commerce is advancing rapidly, and there is a feeling that the urban telephone there cannot be delayed; the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau is also in the process of planning.

The business of Zhejiang Province's long-distance telephones along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road was originally the most developed in Lanxi; the annual turnover was more than 10,000 yuan; followed by Jinhua, reaching more than 7,000 yuan; followed by Qu County, about 5,000 to 6,000 yuan; the other bureaus were between 4,000 to 5,000 yuan and 2,000 yuan. However, since the full line of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway was opened to traffic, Lanxi's business has been declining day by day, while Jinhua's business is booming and has a tendency to replace it. Recently, since the completion of the Jinyu section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the telephone traffic between Longyou, Qu County, and Jiangshan has been progressing at the same time as Jinhua; the most developed long-distance telephones in the past, such as Lanxi, will shift its center of gravity to Jinhua, and Longyou, Qu County, Jiangshan, and others, which were considered insignificant in the past, will be advancing in conjunction with the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway business. The transportation industry is closely related to economic development, and the economic situation of a place changes in prosperity and decline with changes in transportation conditions.

In short, transportation tools complement each other, and the local economy also develops with the transportation industry. Those who are determined to build should be aware of this!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

The Philosophy of the Circle

— Qu Chen

Among all shapes, squares have too many edges and corners; triangles make people think of unharmonious love; length is slow, while shortness is cramped; thickness is heavy, while thinness is frivolous; only the circle is the most complete, the most widely used, and the most popular.

For example, the wheel is round, so it can travel thousands of miles. The door hinge is round, so it can turn easily. The rice bowl is round, which is just right for the mouth. The toilet is round, which fits perfectly to the buttocks. If these things are all changed to squares, then the wheel will not move, the door will not open, the mouth will be sore when eating, and you will feel like sitting on pins and needles when defecating. The embarrassment is indescribable.

Therefore, all useful things are "round for the most important".

Not only in utensils, but also in art. Past poets sang "six inches of round skin with exquisite light." Modern poets sing about "full breasts!" and so on. All worshipers of curved beauty are, in other words, worshipers of "round." The strongest supporter is the ancient Greek mathematician Archimedes, who shouted "Don't ruin my circle" when he was killed by the Romans.

As for being a person, one must speak. Because sharpness is close to meanness, and squares have too many edges and corners, there are times when they are useless. It is never as good as the round's completeness, which follows the way of heaven and can be used in all directions without hindrance.

For example, if you go out occasionally in October weather and suddenly meet a consumptive ghost-like friend who is wearing heavy fur clothes and still saying he is cold, then if he "greets" you, you must not tell him your own experience, saying that the weather is not as cold as he said, because in his feelings, the sky is indeed so cold. If you say an experience that is contrary to his, he will suspect that you are intentionally messing with him. It is best to say, "Ah, the weather is really cold!" You naturally understand in your stomach, but your friend is therefore satisfied and will consider you a "comrade."

Also, if a nearsighted friend insists on calling a sparrow flying in the air an eagle, you must not argue with him about what it is. Because in his vision, it may indeed be an eagle. The result of the argument is that the victory is not necessarily yours, but the breakdown of the relationship is certain.

Here, I think of a typical character.

Shishuo Xinyu quoted Sima Hui's separate biography: "Sima Hui had a humanistic sense of judgment. He lived in Jingzhou and knew that Liu Biao was dark and would harm good people, so he kept silent and did not talk about current affairs. Someone asked Hui about people, but he never distinguished their merits. Every time he said it was good. His wife admonished him, saying, "People are doubtful about quality, you should argue, but you don't say good to everyone, how can people consult you?" Hui said, "As you say, it's also good." The language is quite humorous. This is indeed a good way to preserve life in a well-governed world. De Cao is truly worthy of the title of "Water Mirror." If he had listened to the words of a woman, he would have been a continuation of Kong Beihai Mi Zhengping, who was fond of discussing figures at the time. Therefore, the study of the circle is not to be ignored!

The Misfortune of Women

— Yong

The most miserable people in the world are Chinese women.

Those women from poor families worry about breakfast and then dinner. Emaciated, they beg for food everywhere. I cannot bear to describe their suffering. Their life story is a blurred mess of bloodstains. They are a group abandoned outside of human life by the pressure of history.

Those women from wealthy families, including wives, young mistresses, young ladies, as well as decorative objects and actresses, wear short shorts, long stockings, high heels, expose their bare arms and chests, or naked, fleshy thighs. They go to companies to cut fabric, to dance halls to dance, ride in cars, go to theaters, parks, gambling dens, dog racing tracks, pelota courts... In these places where human desires run rampant, countless modern men accompany them all day long, living carefree lives. I do not want to describe their life story. I do not want to talk about these "gilded parasites."

The fortunate and unfortunate destinies of humanity are thus decided. Every day, when we read the newspaper, we can always find headlines in large characters, using extremely vivid words to describe many scandalous love affairs about women, such as "King of Acrobats and Miss Sun," "The Mermaid and Her Protector"... Records of absolutely no value, or publishing fleshy photos for those concerned to sing and sigh, but there is no cry of the street beggar, no dirty and ragged image! The market is full of fleshly temptations and a torrent of lust, but we cannot hear the curse of life, the miserable cry of death!

People are so fascinated with fleshly and flirtatious things, and they are so enthusiastically promoting Western civilization. In contrast, society uses all its power to oppress the poor and helpless women, forcing them to transform into modern women, sacrificing their looks, or standing on the street corner with tears in their eyes!

How heartbreaking this is!

Although wealthy people are standing on the ground of Western civilization, energetically venting their sexual desires, ordinary poor women also take advantage of the weaknesses of this society. Under the banners of modernity, fitness, etc., there is a dance party today, a fashion exhibition tomorrow, and a beauty contest the day after, with the gimmicks of nude bathing. Chinese women, with no way forward, all move in this direction, begging for the leftovers squandered by those young masters! But China is, after all, a country of ancient civilization. When this wave of Westernized licentiousness rises to its peak, the supporters of the old era, witnessing the signs of national ruin, launch a counterattack of the era, which is to "maintain morality" and promote "propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame."

Yesterday, this newspaper received a telegram from Peiping: "Yuan Liang strictly prohibits dancing... A large number of dancers and male and female patrons were arrested at the Sanchun Dance Hall."

The day before yesterday, the newspaper reported that Nanjing, after banning prostitution, felt that it could not be banned in reality, and then ordered it to be lifted, but the inspection was very strict.

The old capital and the new capital look at women so strictly. The decrees banning dancing and prostitution are so frightening, shaking the hearts of those poor women who sell their art and their bodies. This makes us deeply feel that another kind of sorrow of China's Westernization is to trap Chinese women in an abyss from which they cannot extricate themselves; and to moan painfully in this abyss, without any social sympathy. Society has no politeness or respect for them, only teasing and destruction. The pressure inherited from historical traditions abandons them outside the circle of human life.

Today, these pitiful Chinese women, with no way to make a living, have fallen. This is a fact. But to say that they have destroyed "morality" and lost "propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame" is a great injustice. "Morality" and "propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame" have been swept away by Western ways, and they have also been intoxicated by Western ways. The gentlemen who are banning dancing and prostitution today should first recognize this fact and not praise those who sell their souls to the heavens and beat those who sell their bodies to hell. Those who shout "Long live women's liberation" should also open their eyes to see if this is the era when the misfortune of women has arrived.

Miss Fang

— Shi Ben

Miss Fang of the Kang family returned from a school in Shanghai the other day. Her attire was completely modern, completely different from her appearance as a country girl before. As a result, the neighbors were whispering, "Miss Fang's behavior has changed greatly recently! She's only been in Shanghai for half a year, and she's already behaving strangely. It's clear that Shanghai is a bad place! No wonder her aunt said that she went to Shanghai to study, but in reality, she just wanted to pick up a gigolo in Shanghai to be her husband. Now, looking at her 'Westernized' appearance, her aunt's words are definitely true. Alas! What a good girl, to have changed so much, it's really a pity!" Most of the neighbors have an 18th-century perspective, and they cannot help but regard Miss Fang's lively behavior and fashionable dress as irregular. Moreover, they often listen to the fifth aunt, who opposes Miss Fang, and her words that damage Miss Fang's reputation. So, now everyone is unanimously criticizing Miss Fang in this way. It turns out that Miss Fang is the youngest daughter of Mr. Kang. Her mother is Mr. Kang's fourth concubine. She was born with a charming appearance and a graceful figure. Her bright black eyes and two intoxicatingly charming dimples add to her beautiful demeanor. Therefore, the young masters in X Town are all infatuated and eagerly come to the Kang residence to propose marriage. However, her parents regard her as the apple of their eye and love her extremely, so how could they easily promise her to someone? As a result, she has been kept at home until the age of eighteen and has not yet been selected. Although she is accustomed to being spoiled, her temperament is very gentle, and her demeanor is also generous. Because she grew up in the countryside, where customs are old-fashioned, she has been hidden in her boudoir since she was a child and has not left her house. All her actions are completely in the style of an 18th-century lady. Mr. Kang often opposes modern women going to school, saying that it is outrageous for men and women to mix together. "A woman without talent is virtuous." What is the use of learning? Therefore, Miss Fang has not received any education until the age of eighteen and has no knowledge in her mind. As a result, people call her "an embroidered pillow!" Unfortunately, in the spring of last year, Miss Fang's mother suddenly fell ill and died! Two months later, her father married a fifth concubine, who came from a brothel, had a romantic temperament, and a frivolous demeanor. Her tolerance was also very narrow. Whether it was eating or wearing, she was stingy and calculating, so as soon as she entered the house, she and Miss Fang became like fire and water and often had conflicts. Behind her back, she also instigated Mr. Kang to be cold to his daughter. Mr. Kang was originally a confused idiot and only loved beauty, so he immediately overturned his usual love for his daughter and scolded Miss Fang every day. The fifth concubine secretly added various restrictions and oppressions to Miss Fang's diet and expenses. At this time, Miss Fang was extremely sad. She thought of how much her mother loved her when she was alive and how comfortable her life was. Now that her mother is dead, and a "concubine" has been brought in, her father looks down on her and she has suffered all kinds of cruel oppressions. So, how can she survive if things continue like this day after day? Moreover, she does not know a single word, and she has no knowledge at all. Won't the marriage problem in the future also be hindered? In addition, the fifth concubine opposes her, and the marriage that her father makes will definitely not have good results! It is better to take advantage of the fact that she cannot live in peace at home and go to the outside world to study for a few years. With knowledge, she can make her own decisions in everything. When she thought of this, she felt extremely sad and could not help but sob. But, when she thought again that staying at home was not a good idea, she left home in the summer of that year and went to study at XX Girls' School in Shanghai. Since Miss Fang went to Shanghai to study, the fifth concubine often talked to people, saying, "When a girl gets older, her mind will become active. There are many beautiful people in Shanghai. She is going to recruit a young official! Otherwise, she is already eighteen years old. Why is she still going to school? Isn't it like 'playing drums and trumpets at the school when she's eighty years old, with a short life and short breath'? Alas! A lady from a wealthy family is so shameless and goes to Shanghai to pretend to study. It's really a shame to the Kang family!" So, this time, when Miss Fang came back from a school in Shanghai, the neighbors said that her "behavior had changed greatly."

On the Standards of "Feminine Beauty"

— Li Yue

Whether it is in a feudal society or a capitalist society, as long as it is a system centered on men, women are often regarded as commodities or playthings. Since women are regarded as commodities or playthings, there is naturally a distinction between superior and inferior, beautiful and ugly. In our China, women in this kind of society used to take absolute "morbid" conditions as the standard of superior beauty. Therefore, the typical woman under this standard must have a waist like a "willow branch," "golden lotus" feet, a "melon seed" face, and "sheep fat" skin. In addition, the chest should be flat, the head should be lowered, the hands should be small and thin, and the legs should be thin and weak; the eyes should be fixed as if they contain a bag of autumn water, and the cheeks should often fly with shy red clouds; they should also be melancholic and sickly, too weak to wear clothes, and even a gust of wind seems to blow them away... This means that the thinner the better, the sicker the more beautiful; the names "sick beauty" and "thin beauty" are born like this. However, the lifestyle of these "beauties" and "fair women" is very simple, they are just long-term slaves of men.

In recent years, the storm of Europe and the United States has swept across the entire mainland of China, penetrating the hearts of every man and woman in China. The standards of excellence and beauty for women, no, commodities and playthings, have been drastically transformed from "morbid" conditions to complete "flirtatiousness"! Standing at the forefront of this storm and calling themselves women of the era, they have all fully expressed their flirtatiousness and charm under this modern new standard of "enchanting." Thus, the heels are higher, the buttocks are twisted, the thighs are bare, the hair is curled, and the eyebrows are shaved and redrawn so thin, so long, and so black; the lips are like blood, the breasts are trembling, and the face is no different from a monkey's buttocks... This means that the more enchanting the more beautiful, the more charming the more valuable! Really, the facts show it, especially in Shanghai, which is full of foreigners, it is expressed most thoroughly; many serious things, as well as many things of promotion and wealth, success and prosperity, are mostly for or rely on this flirtatiousness! This charm! So, naturally, this flirtatiousness becomes a commodity in one aspect and is regarded as a plaything in another. But their lifestyles are different from "long-term slaves of men"; they can blow smoke rings, eat candied chestnuts and chocolate all day long, go to companies to cut fabrics, go to dance halls to dance, ride in cars, and go to foreign houses, parks, theaters, gambling dens, dog racing tracks, pelota courts... In these frenzied places where human desires run rampant, there are always large groups of idle modern men like gentlemen accompanying them on carefree outings. They are gilded!

...Whether in the past or now, this expression is undoubtedly deformed! All are crazy! Brutal! Cruel!

However, women, the woman as a commodity and a plaything in a contradictory society and a decadent system, is there no other way for them to express their rational beauty besides the deformed "morbid" conditions and the crazy "flirtatiousness"? How unfortunate this is!

A few days ago, I saw a sex education film in "Shanghai". This film is showing another type of feminine beauty, which is the health and beauty of those active and progressive women in a rational system in a society that is absolutely different from ours. Everything in the society there is different from ours; they have no "morbid" conditions, and they have no "flirtatiousness"; they are not thin, not weak, not charming, not delicate, not deformed, and not crazy; their lives are full of boiling blood, the flame of youth, active spirits, and healthy bodies; they are happily and peacefully speeding along a rational and correct path, rushing forward by leaps and bounds towards a bright and pure circle! Driving thousands of miles a day!

This really makes me feel sad and sorrowful for our women! Are we really going to harden our hearts and let our nation degenerate into a terrible situation from which it will never recover? Gentlemen engaged in the women's movement: please, is the task under your shouts of "long live" and the call of bright flags to turn women into deformed and crazy "morbid" and "flirtatious" beings? Or should they be turned into active, progressive, and healthy women? These must be clearly recognized before we can answer our questions with facts.

To Lili

— Zheng Qing

Lili:

We have only known each other for a short two years, but I already have a very deep understanding of you. Lili, I really love you. I love your sensibility, your quick wit, your lively manners, I love your straightforwardness, your arrogance, I love the accuracy of your thoughts, and even more I love that you have simple virtues and no shameful coquettishness. You have a delicate and sweet heart, a gentle mind, and no romantic vulgarity. You have the appearance and substance of a truly modern woman, but you have not been corrupted by the so-called modernity of the outside world. Lili, I love you deeply and tirelessly.

But in recent months, your cold and insulting treatment of me has given me great pain. Ah! Lili, is my understanding of you wrong? Lili, are you also like ordinary women with common views? If so, how deep is the pain you have given me; how long will it take to heal? Oh! I know, a poor boy like me is simply not worthy of loving any girl. Can a poor boy also have the good fortune to indulge in love? Love is fundamentally based on money. But, Lili, I don't think of you as such a woman. I want to respect your female personality. You are a high school student, and I don't believe that you would be willing to lower your own personality! If so, what kind of education have you received? Isn't the education you received like whitewashing a wall? Isn't your entry into school just a step towards seduction? It is called a high school student in name, but in reality, it is just a charming

Page 23

fellow who likes to sacrifice everything under mercenary marriage? Writing to this point, the previous scenes have become active in my mind again. Alas! Lili, is it true that women always like shiny money? My heart feels as cold as if I have drunk ice.

Lili, I tell you, in this era of transition between the old and the new, young people who are in such an environment, if they want not to be controlled by the environment, then they must take out their own willpower to fight against this hateful environment. We must control this environment; we certainly do not need to be attached to or sad about the past, but we also do not need to yearn for the future. We only need to grasp reality, only reality is the most reliable. Lili! I hope you will take my words and experience them.

Recently, I learned that you are troubled in your heart. Lili, your heart is so contradictory that it is pitiful. Lili, but you must recognize that even if your own environment makes you troubled, you still have to fight against it, let alone your so-called objective environment!

The time has matured to this point, we have talked about everything, so I hope very much that you can tell me your difficulties. I can tell you directly and happily that I am a poor boy who is completely destitute, but I do not hope to get rich. I only hope that I can stand at the forefront of the era. At least we cannot fall behind. We must fulfill the responsibilities that we young people should bear. We must recognize the shortcomings of society and correct them. Talking to this point, it can be considered a paragraph. I hope you, I hope you very much, think again and again, experience again and again. I am always praying for you like this. You are a high school student. You are responsible for transformation. You always have to supervise

Yourself. Sincerely, December 19th night

Amateur Mailbox

Better Late Than Never

Editor:

Please forgive me for disturbing your peace of mind in your busy schedule. However, how can I not do so? The fact is this: I, a junior high school student, had to give up my schooling life due to economic constraints. Not long after, I took on the job of a debt collector in a company. My monthly salary is still enough to make ends meet. As the saying goes: "When a son is old, he should get married; when a daughter is old, she should get married." My father saw my age increasing little by little, but the saying "When a son is old, he should get married" had not yet been put into practice. However, without any savings, how can we afford a wedding in this society dominated by money? However, if we don't do it, we are afraid that people will laugh at us, saying, "Such a big son, and he hasn't started a family yet." Because of this, we borrowed five hundred yuan from someone and married a wife, who is also my wife. With one more person, of course, expenses will increase a lot. The burden becomes heavier day by day, and there is no guarantee of paying back the five hundred yuan for the wedding. It really fits the saying: "What you are marrying is borrowed, what you are sleeping with is debt." We are still living frugally. What if we have children? Wouldn't expenses increase again? Wouldn't the burden be even heavier?

Kind editor! I sincerely ask you to solve this problem that I think is difficult for me. And please tell me, why do people treat marrying off their daughters like doing business? Very sincerely waiting for your reply, Mr. Editor. The end. I wish you peace. Bowing respectfully, Liang Niangdai

Editor's note: The last question raised by Mr. Liang is, "Why do people treat marrying off their daughters like doing business?" This question is easy to answer, but it is also very difficult to solve. This is of course caused by the entire bad society at present, and it is not something that a few people can do, nor is it something that a few people can improve. For us ordinary people, it is not to destroy our ambition, but we are powerless, so we don't need to talk about changing customs and habits. The best way for us to deal with this bad environment is to adopt a firm and clear approach; if you want to do business well, I will not come to make you successful, let's see what you can do. Unfortunately, Mr. Liang and his parents do not have this spirit, and even passive resistance cannot be done. As a result, they are dragged into the water by the evil society and fall into the sea of ​​misery. Since this is a fait accompli, repentance is too late. The only way to remedy it is to make up for it. On the active side, of course, we must work hard to increase income; knowledge, experience, and the full use of opportunities are all important. On the passive side, of course, we must seek to save on expenses; clothing, food, housing, and transportation all need to be tightened. And it is best to practice birth control in the near future, when you are still young and there is no way to produce. After practicing birth control, you should comply with the difficulties. As for the appropriate method of birth control, you should plan in name. In the middle, it is not only unreliable, but also very dangerous. And for the sake of living, few people can use it in a good way.

Novel

Shanghai (29)

— Zhang Laosan

(42) I Understand

The situation in Shanghai grows tenser by the day, with people panicking as if a major war is about to break out. In the Chinese-controlled areas, trunks, luggage, and citizens are crowding into the foreign concessions in a confused mass, as if a shell will explode on their behinds if they are a step too late. Due to successive civil wars, the citizens have become accustomed to seeking protection under the foreign powers of imperialism. The population within the concessions has increased, and housing prices have soared, partly due to the war.

Our school has been suspended, the magazine has stopped publication, everything has come to a standstill, except that we still have to eat every day.

This afternoon, my maternal uncle Xu Bingnan's daughter, my cousin Xu Huijin, sent a carload of luggage to the office. She asked if there was a place to store it temporarily, until her father rented a house and could move it there.

"Is Uncle still at Xujiahui?"

"Father wasn't planning to flee," my cousin nodded. "But today the driver, A'gen, said that Japanese soldiers had already occupied XX Academy. However, Father's health can't handle too much exertion. He wanted me to deposit the valuables with you first and leave when the situation becomes more critical."

"That's good." I called out loudly to A'fu, "Help A'gen move the luggage to the third floor."

"The third floor? Where should we put it?"

"Sister Min has left, her room is empty."

"Fled to the countryside? Such a tiny bit of courage!" She laughed, and I laughed too.

"Let's talk after the luggage is moved," Xiao Huang's voice was so loud.

A'fu helped A'gen move the luggage to the third floor. The normally tidy bedroom now looked like a cargo hold. There was no trace left of the free-spirited woman, but Hui was still behind the scenes.

The three of them came downstairs to our bedroom. Xiao Huang, no longer like an ugly daughter-in-law afraid to meet her in-laws, was the first to speak.

"Miss Xu, you should have driven Sun Min away long ago!"

"Mr. Huang, you are lost in your fantasies again." My cousin still thought Xiao Huang wouldn't say anything serious and teased him playfully.

"Hmph! You insult me!" He raised his fist and waved it in the air, as if to knock down some target.

I remained silent. My cousin ignored Xiao Huang.

"When did Min leave?" she asked me.

"Almost a month ago, wasn't it?"

My cousin looked suspiciously at Xiao Huang's face, which was taut like a drum.

"Because of a letter from you!" A bombshell exploded.

"Brother?"

"Just two lines of pencil writing," I replied blandly.

"That wasn't what I expected," Sister Hui said softly. "Ever since Mr. Huang joked with her that day, Min came to Xujiahui. She said she was a woman who could not marry, she would not fall in love, because she didn't recognize herself as a woman. Such jokes became commonplace. Later, when you fell ill, we had many opportunities to talk, and Min never revealed her feelings." Sister Hui paused, then looked at Xiao Huang's face again, and continued: "Brother, there is no room for a third party on the path of love. Since that is the case, I have decided to find Min and bring her back. I don't want to do something that someone else doesn't want." Sister Hui stood up as if to leave.

"Miss Xu, what time is it now? This is not the time for love. Sun Min will definitely not come back. If we have the opportunity, we should do something to help the country and show the strength of our people." Xiao Huang said each word slowly, as if preparing the wording of the next sentence while speaking the previous one. Usually, with such an attitude, my cousin would have laughed first.

This was the first time I saw her serious face. After listening to Xiao Huang's words, she didn't speak for a long time. Finally, she stood up and said, "I understand."

"Our comrade!" Xiao Huang's hand shot up, his heels clicking together.

Home
